## 10. Metric Ownership

10.1 Names

### Owner
Recruitment Intelligence.

### Consumers
Partner Intelligence.
Forecast Intelligence.
Business Planning.
Mick.

### Non-owners
Compensation, Productivity, Career, Advisor Experience.


10.2 Sources

### Owner
Recruitment Intelligence for observed source assignment.
Rule Pack for source taxonomy definitions and targets.

### Consumers
Partner Intelligence, Forecast Intelligence, Business Planning.

### Non-owners
Compensation, Productivity, UI.


10.3 Interviews

### Owner
Recruitment Intelligence.

### Metrics
EI, ES, EC, EA scheduled and completed.

### Consumers
Partner Intelligence, Forecast Intelligence, Business Planning, Mick.

### Non-owners
Compensation, Career, Conservation.


10.4 Conversions

### Owner
Recruitment Intelligence.

### Metrics
Name to EI.
EI to ES.
ES to EC.
EC to EA.
EA to connected.
Connected to signed as consumed from Precontract or transition outcome.

### Consumers
Forecast Intelligence, Partner Intelligence, Business Planning.

### Non-owners
Compensation, Productivity, Advisor Experience.


10.5 Connected

### Owner
Boundary ownership.
Recruitment owns candidate conversion to connected as recruitment outcome.
Precontract owns operational lifecycle after connected.

### Consumers
Partner Intelligence, Forecast Intelligence, Business Planning, Compensation after downstream rule interpretation.

### Non-owners
UI, Mick, Advisor Experience.


10.6 Signed

### Owner
Precontract/Career boundary for official contract event.
Recruitment consumes signed status for conversion quality.

### Consumers
Recruitment, Partner Intelligence, Career Intelligence, Compensation.

### Non-owners
Recruitment must not own official advisor identity after signing.


10.7 PM

### Owner
Recruitment Intelligence.

### Metrics
PM referrals created.
PM referral conversion.
PM network depth.
PM quality by originating candidate.

### Consumers
Partner Intelligence, Forecast Intelligence, Business Planning, Relationship Intelligence.

### Non-owners
Compensation unless Rule Pack defines attribution/bonus interpretation.


10.8 Time by stage

### Owner
Recruitment Intelligence for recruitment stages.
Precontract for precontract stages.

### Consumers
Forecast Intelligence, Business Planning, Partner Intelligence, Mick.

### Non-owners
Compensation, UI.


10.9 Risk

### Owner
Recruitment Intelligence for recruitment risks.

### Consumers
Partner Intelligence, Business Planning, Manager Intelligence, Advisor Experience if surfaced contextually.

### Non-owners
Forecast may forecast risk but should not own recruitment risk facts.


10.10 Source quality

### Owner
Recruitment Intelligence.

### Consumers
Partner Intelligence, Business Planning, Forecast Intelligence.

### Non-owners
Forge Core, Compensation, Productivity.


## 11. Recruitment Network

Recruitment Network should exist formally.

### Value

It captures the fact that recruitment is not only a linear funnel.

Candidates, advisors, centers of influence and partners generate networks.

### Example

Juan refers Pedro.
Pedro refers Ana.
Ana becomes Partner.

This matters because Juan may have created large network value even if Juan never signed.

Should it persist?

Yes, but as relationship and attribution history, not as a separate duplicate identity graph.

### What decisions it enables

Which candidates generate valuable networks.
Which advisors are strong recruiting nodes.
Which centers of influence deserve attention.
Which Partner is building referral loops.
Which source has hidden downstream value.
Which candidate deserves follow-up because of network quality.

### Risks

Privacy.
Consent.
Incorrect attribution.
Overvaluing network size over quality.
Duplicated identities.
Treating social connection as commercial permission.
Compensation disputes if network attribution is later monetized.

### Guardrails

Use CommercialRelationship for relationships.
Use CommercialAttribution for credit when applicable.
Use EvidenceRecord for source.
Use RuleSnapshot for any monetized interpretation.
Separate network value from compensation.


## 12. Causal Chain

### Official causal chain

Sources
Names
EI
ES
EC
EA
Connected
Signed
Development
TA
Qualified
Productivity
Compensation


12.1 Leading indicators

Warm-source names.
Total names.
P200 completion.
Magic Question asked.
PM referrals generated.
EI scheduled.
EI completed.
Stage movement velocity.
Follow-up consistency.
Source mix quality.
Candidate response behavior.


12.2 Lagging indicators

Connected candidates.
Signed candidates.
Developed advisors.
TA outcomes.
Qualified advisors.
Productivity.
Partner compensation.
Alta Partner.


12.3 Root causes

### Low names
Prospecting/source activation problem.

### Low warm sources
Network activation problem.

### High FF dependency
Warm market weakness or partner behavior issue.

Many names, few EI:
Contact/follow-up quality or source quality problem.

Many EI, few ES:
Initial filtering or opportunity framing problem.

Many ES, few EC:
Selection fit or process discipline problem.

Many EC, few EA:
Career conviction or follow-up problem.

Many EA, few connected:
Commitment/precontract readiness problem.

### Connected but not signed
Precontract execution problem.

### Signed but not developed
Development ownership problem.


12.4 False indicators

Many names without interviews.
Many PM referrals without conversion.
P200 completed but no contact activity.
Cold-source volume without warm-source mix.
Connected candidates without signed contracts.
Signed advisors without development.
Forecasted signings shown as actual signings.


12.5 Vanity metrics

Raw names.
Raw P200 count.
Raw PM count.
Interview count without conversion.
Source count without quality.
Network size without downstream movement.


## 13. Red Team Review

### Scenario 1
200 names and zero interviews.

### Model response
P200/name volume is not recruitment health.
Recruitment must flag conversion failure from name to EI.

### What breaks
Only volume-based model breaks.

### Guardrail
Measure conversion and next action, not only names.


### Scenario 2
100 FF and zero CI.

### Model response
Source mix risk and warm-source shortage.

### What breaks
Any model that treats all names equally.

### Guardrail
Source Quality Model and Rule Pack source targets.


### Scenario 3
Much PM but bad quality.

### Model response
PM network volume is not PM network value.

### What breaks
PM as simple source count.

### Guardrail
Measure PM downstream conversion and origin candidate quality.


### Scenario 4
Connected without signed.

### Model response
Connected and signed remain separate lifecycle events.

### What breaks
Any model that treats connected as final recruiting success.

### Guardrail
Precontract boundary and distinct events.


### Scenario 5
Signed without developed.

### Model response
Recruitment succeeded at signing but downstream development risk exists.

### What breaks
Recruitment-only success definition.

### Guardrail
Recruitment feeds Development but does not own Development.


### Scenario 6
Partner stops recruiting for one year.

### Model response
Leading indicators collapse before compensation collapses.

### What breaks
Lagging-only manager dashboard.

### Guardrail
Business Planning and Partner Intelligence consume recruiting leading indicators.


### Scenario 7
Duplicated candidate.

### Model response
CommercialPerson identity resolution required.

### What breaks
Spreadsheet row identity.

### Guardrail
Capture Once and duplicate detection.


### Scenario 8
Manager change.

### Model response
CommercialAssignment history preserves responsibility by period.

### What breaks
Current manager overwrite.

### Guardrail
Time-bounded assignments.


### Scenario 9
Partner change.

### Model response
CommercialAssignment and CommercialAttribution separate responsibility from credit.

### What breaks
Single partner field.

### Guardrail
Historical assignment plus attribution.


### Scenario 10
Candidate never signs but generates great network.

### Model response
RecruitmentNetwork preserves candidate network value.

### What breaks
Signed-only candidate value model.

### Guardrail
Magic Question Network Model.


### Missing guardrails

Official POP definition.
Rule Pack source target definitions.
Precontract transition ownership.
Privacy and consent rules for recruitment network.
Evidence quality requirements for imported Excel data.
Clear ownership of P200 universal primitive.


## 14. Foundation Compatibility

14.1 CommercialPerson

Compatible.

RecruitmentCandidate must be a role/context over CommercialPerson.

### Conflict
If RecruitmentCandidate becomes durable identity, foundation is violated.


14.2 CommercialAccount

Compatible.

Recruitment may not always need CommercialAccount, but business, family or center-of-influence recruitment paths may use it.

### Conflict
None immediate.


14.3 CommercialRelationship

Compatible and required.

Used for referrals, nominations, PM, CI and network edges.

### Conflict
Relationship must not imply attribution or compensation automatically.


14.4 CommercialAssignment

Compatible and required.

Used for Partner/manager responsibility over candidate pipeline by period.

### Conflict
Do not use assignment as attribution.


14.5 CommercialAttribution

Compatible and required.

Used for referral origin, PM origin, connection credit and possible Partner credit.

### Conflict
Attribution must not imply payment without Rule Pack.


14.6 EvidenceRecord

Compatible and required.

Used for Excel import, manual capture, interview notes, P200, PM and source assignment.

### Conflict
Manual spreadsheet data may have low confidence unless provenance is preserved.


14.7 ProvenanceRecord

Compatible and required.

### Used to explain how data entered Forge

Excel.
Manual input.
Manager input.
Candidate-provided referral.
Imported report.

### Conflict
None.


14.8 RuleSnapshot

Compatible and required.

### Used for

Source targets.
Warm-source thresholds.
POP definitions.
Stage expectations.
Recruitment activity standards.
Downstream Partner compensation interpretations.

### Conflict
Hardcoding SMNYL rules into Core would violate Foundation Lock.


14.9 PeriodSnapshot

Compatible and required.

### Used for

Weekly recruiting period.
Monthly recruiting period.
Quarter planning period.
Precontract window.
Partner compensation quarter.

### Conflict
Recruitment month, weekly RTW cadence and Partner quarter must not be mixed.


## 15. Final Verdict

### Status
ARCHITECTURE CANDIDATE

### Why not FOUNDATION DRAFT
The domain is more mature than a draft because PAQ-01 reviewed real operational artifacts and this model defines boundaries, entities, relationships, events, metrics and foundation compatibility.

### Why not ARCHITECTURE LOCK
### Three items remain unresolved

1. POP definition is not confirmed.
2. PCV Partner 2026 rules were not text-extractable in this pass.
3. SMNYL Agency 2026 Rule Pack needs formal recruitment rules for targets, source warmth, stage expectations and downstream Partner interpretation.

### What is approved

Recruitment Intelligence as a formal Intelligence Phase domain.
RecruitmentCandidate as a recruitment context over CommercialPerson.
Recruitment Source Quality Model.
Magic Question Network Model.
Recruitment Network as a formal conceptual model.
Recruitment funnel ownership.
Recruitment event taxonomy.
Recruitment metric ownership.
P200 as market evidence consumed by Recruitment, not recruitment-only list.

### What is not approved

Implementation.
Engines.
Schemas.
UI.
Hardcoded SMNYL thresholds in Core.
Compensation calculations.
POP interpretation without source rule.

### Final architectural statement

Recruitment Intelligence is the domain that tells Forge whether a Partner is creating future advisor capacity.

### It must protect the difference between

Names and quality.
Volume and conversion.
Referral count and network value.
Connected and signed.
Recruitment and precontract.
Signing and development.
Forecast and fact.
Rule Pack interpretation and Core primitive.

This model is sufficient to proceed to a formal Recruitment Intelligence Architecture document or Rule Pack recruitment hardening pass.

It is not sufficient for implementation lock.



===== PAQ-02-RECRUITMENT-DOMAIN-MODEL-ADDENDUM.md =====

# PAQ-02 Recruitment Domain Model Addendum

## Repository References

- [FORGE_MASTER_BUILD_TREE.md](FORGE_MASTER_BUILD_TREE.md)
- [AGENTS.md](AGENTS.md)
- [FORGE_CONSTITUTION_V3.md](FORGE_CONSTITUTION_V3.md)
- [FORGE_FOUNDATION_LOCK.md](FORGE_FOUNDATION_LOCK.md)

---


### New evidence reviewed

ES Leccion 1.pdf
ES Leccion 2.pdf
ES Leccion 3.pdf

### Reviewed locations

/storage/emulated/0/Download/Quick Share/ES Leccion 1.pdf
/storage/emulated/0/Download/Quick Share/ES Leccion 2.pdf
/storage/emulated/0/Download/Quick Share/ES Leccion 3.pdf

### Purpose
Delta analysis only.

This document does not rewrite PAQ-02.
This document does not create code.
This document does not create engines.
This document does not create schemas.
This document does not modify UI.
This document does not commit changes.


## 1. Confirmed Assumptions

1.1 Recruitment Intelligence is a valid Intelligence Phase domain.

Confirmed.

The training material confirms that prospecting is not an optional activity.
It describes prospecting as the central or root activity of the sales cycle.

ES Leccion 3 establishes that prospecting is the point of departure for the entire sales cycle and that the cycle must keep turning continuously.

### Impact
Recruitment Intelligence remains a valid domain and becomes even more important than PAQ-02 originally stated.


1.2 Recruitment is not merely a spreadsheet funnel.

Confirmed.

The training material frames the advisor career as a relationship-based commercial system.

### It repeatedly emphasizes

Community relationships.
Natural groups.
Networks.
Referrals.
Centers of Influence.
Market Natural.
Prospecting discipline.

### Impact
PAQ-02 correctly rejected copying Reclutamiento.xlsx and correctly moved toward domain semantics.


1.3 P200 is not only recruitment.

Confirmed.

### The training documents describe a broader concept

Market Natural.
Proyecto de Marketing.
People known by the advisor.
Groups where the advisor belongs.
Relationship inventory.
Natural markets.

The workbook P200 aligns with this broader structure.

### Impact
PAQ-02 was correct to say that P200 should not be treated as recruitment-only.


1.4 Magic Question is not just a source.

Confirmed.

The training material repeatedly describes referrals and networks as compounding.

It states that people know more people and that referrals can produce an effectively continuous source of prospects.

### Impact
### PAQ-02 was correct to model PM as

Source.
Loop.
Network.
Activity.
Event.
Metric source.


1.5 Recruitment Network should be first-class.

Confirmed.

The training material validates that referral chains and centers of influence are structurally important, not incidental.

### It describes

People referring people.
Centers of Influence opening access to groups.
Referrals creating trust before contact.
Groups leading to more groups.
Objects or situations triggering people.

### Impact
Recruitment Network remains required.


1.6 Recruitment Risk should be first-class.

Confirmed.

The training material explicitly describes the roller coaster effect caused by stopping prospecting.

It shows that failure to prospect today creates future absence of people to contact, future stress and future sales inconsistency.

### Impact
Recruitment Risk should remain a first-class interpretation model.


1.7 Inactivity predicts future productivity decline.

Confirmed.

The roller coaster example confirms that prospecting inactivity has delayed consequences.

The absence of current prospecting does not always hurt current sales immediately.
It hurts future appointments, future presentations, future closes and future production.

### Impact
Recruitment activity is a leading indicator of future productivity.


1.8 Forecasting future talent shortage from recruiting behavior is valid.

Confirmed with guardrail.

Forge can forecast risk of future talent shortage or future pipeline shortage from:

Low prospecting activity.
Low name creation.
Weak source mix.
Weak referral activity.
Low P200/Market Natural depth.
Low appointment creation.

### Guardrail
Forecast remains suggestion, not fact.


## 2. Invalid Assumptions

2.1 Recruitment begins with a name.

Invalidated.

The training material shows that recruitment/prospecting begins before a name is entered.

### It begins with

Relationships.
Community membership.
Groups.
Market Natural.
Known people.
People connected to other people.
Centers of Influence.
Objects and situations that reveal people.

### Required correction
The canonical upstream chain should not begin with Name.

It should begin with Relationship Capital.

### Corrected chain

Relationship Capital
Market Natural
Community / Group
Person known or reachable
Name
Prospect
Candidate


2.2 P200 is primarily a recruitment artifact.

Invalidated.

P200 is better understood as a concrete artifact of Market Natural / Proyecto de Marketing.

It can feed recruitment, but it is not only recruitment.

### Required correction
PAQ-02 should explicitly state that Recruitment consumes P200 as evidence of relationship capital and market capacity.


2.3 Recruitment creates relationship capital.

Partially invalidated.

Recruitment can expand relationship capital, especially through referrals and Magic Question.

But the training material shows that Recruitment mostly consumes pre-existing relationship capital:

Family.
Friends.
Community.
Past associations.
Current associations.
Centers of Influence.
Groups.
Service providers.
Professional networks.

### Required correction
Recruitment Intelligence should be modeled as a consumer and activator of Relationship Capital, not the original owner of all relationship capital.


2.4 Source taxonomy is sufficient to explain origin.

Partially invalidated.

NOM, CI, RDA, OP, PM and FF are useful operational source labels, but official training material shows deeper structures underneath sources:

Relationship type.
Community group.
Trust path.
Familiarity.
Influence.
Need segment.
Network path.
Market Natural.

### Required correction
Source model should include relationship context, not only source code.


2.5 P200 completion alone indicates market strength.

Invalidated or at least weakened.

Training material explicitly notes that the size of the list is important, but what the advisor does with the names matters more.

### Required correction
P200 should be evaluated by activation, classification, contactability, relationship quality, referral potential and downstream conversion.


## 3. New Architectural Discoveries

3.1 Relationship precedes name.

### Discovery
The training material establishes that the advisor's career is based on relationships with people.

### Architecture implication
RecruitmentCandidate should not be the first conceptual primitive in the funnel.

The upstream primitive is relationship access.

### Corrected conceptual flow

Relationship
Community / Group
Market Natural
Person
Name
Prospect
Candidate
Interview
Connected
Signed


3.2 Market Natural is relationship capital.

### Discovery
Market Natural is not merely a prospect list.

It is the advisor's initial relationship capital:

People known.
Groups joined.
Past associations.
Current associations.
Professional/community access.
People who recognize the advisor's name.

### Architecture implication
P200 / Proyecto de Marketing should be interpreted as evidence of relationship capital.


3.3 Things mean people.

### Discovery
Training material explicitly teaches that "people mean people" and "things mean people."

### Meaning
Recruitment opportunity can be triggered not only by explicit referrals, but also by objects, situations, places, employers, events, family facts, service providers and organizations.

### Architecture implication
Recruitment Intelligence needs signal extraction from relationship context.

### Examples

Mentioned employer.
Mentioned school.
Mentioned club.
Mentioned doctor.
Mentioned jewelry store.
Mentioned promotion.
Mentioned new baby.
Mentioned service provider.

These are not candidates yet.
They are prospecting triggers.


3.4 Centers of Influence are relationship amplifiers.

### Discovery
CI is not just a source label.

A Center of Influence is a respected person who can influence actions of others and open access to groups.

### Architecture implication
CI should be modeled as a relationship node with influence quality, group access and trust transfer.


3.5 Referral trust is causal.

### Discovery
Training material states that referrals matter because they create attention, pre-establish value and transfer trust before first contact.

### Architecture implication
Source Quality Model should include trust transfer as a causal factor, not only a descriptive tag.


3.6 Prospecting is the root rhythm of production.

### Discovery
The roller coaster effect proves that prospecting has delayed impact.

### Architecture implication
Recruitment Risk and Productivity Risk are causally linked through time.

Inactivity today can forecast pipeline shortage later.


3.7 Career Capital is real as a concept.

### Discovery
The training material supports a higher-order concept beyond Recruitment:

Career Capital.

### Possible components

Market Natural.
Community membership.
Group access.
Centers of Influence.
Referrals.
Relationship graph.
Social graph.
Professional graph.
Trust capital.
Familiarity.
Need segmentation knowledge.

### Architecture implication
Recruitment Intelligence appears to consume Career Capital.

### However
This addendum should not create a new domain.

It should mark Career Capital as a discovered higher-order concept requiring architectural evaluation before formal adoption.


## 4. Required Changes to Paq-02

4.1 Change the upstream funnel definition.

### Current PAQ-02 tendency
Source
Name
P200 / market evidence
EI
ES
EC
EA
Connected
Signed

### Required delta
### Add upstream relationship layer

Relationship Capital
Community / Group
Market Natural
Person known or reachable
Name
Prospect
Candidate
EI
ES
EC
EA
Connected
Signed


4.2 Update RecruitmentCandidate boundary.

### Required delta
RecruitmentCandidate should begin when a person enters a recruitment process.

Before that, the person may be:

CommercialPerson.
Relationship node.
Market Natural contact.
Referral possibility.
Prospecting trigger.
P200 entry.

Not every relationship or name is a RecruitmentCandidate.


4.3 Update P200 semantics.

### Required delta
### P200 should be described as

Evidence of Market Natural.
Evidence of relationship capital.
Input to Recruitment Intelligence.
Leading indicator of future prospecting capacity.
Possible activity artifact.
Possible snapshot.

It should not be owned exclusively by Recruitment Intelligence.


4.4 Update Source Model.

### Required delta
### Source should include

Source label.
Relationship path.
Trust transfer.
Community/group origin.
Influence node.
Referral chain.
Familiarity.
Evidence.

NOM, CI, RDA, OP, PM and FF are not enough by themselves.


4.5 Strengthen Magic Question Network Model.

### Required delta
PM should be treated as a network-generation mechanism, not merely a source code.

Magic Question creates graph expansion.

### The value of PM should be measured by

Referral count.
Referral quality.
Referral depth.
Conversion.
Trust transfer.
Network continuation.


4.6 Add Prospecting Trigger concept.

### Required delta
Recruitment Intelligence needs a concept for signals that reveal people before they become names.

### Examples

People mentioned in conversation.
Organizations mentioned.
Service providers mentioned.
New job.
Promotion.
Baby.
Club membership.
School group.
Professional group.

This is the architectural implication of "things mean people."


4.7 Promote Recruitment Risk.

### Required delta
Recruitment Risk should be first-class in PAQ-02.

### It should include

Name shortage risk.
Warm relationship shortage risk.
Prospecting inactivity risk.
Roller coaster risk.
Stage bottleneck risk.
Network depletion risk.
P200 unactivated risk.
Referral failure risk.


4.8 Add delayed-effect clocks.

### Required delta
PAQ-02 should recognize that recruitment behavior has delayed consequences.

Current inactivity may not show in current production.
It can show later as future appointment shortage, future candidate shortage, future advisor shortage and future productivity shortage.

Recruitment Intelligence therefore needs future risk windows.


4.9 Clarify Relationship Intelligence dependency.

### Required delta
Recruitment Intelligence consumes Relationship Capital and relationship graph context.

It may create new relationship edges through PM, referrals and CI.

But it should not own the full relationship graph.


4.10 Keep Career Capital as discovered, not ratified.

### Required delta
PAQ-02 should mention Career Capital as a discovered candidate concept.

It should not declare it a locked domain yet.


## 5. New Domains Discovered

5.1 Relationship Graph / Relationship Capital

### Discovery status
Strongly indicated.

### Evidence
Training material repeatedly states that the career is based on relationships, groups, community, people knowing people and referrals.

### Possible responsibility
Represent social, professional, family, community and influence relationships that exist before a specific recruitment, sales or revenue process.

### Relationship to Recruitment
Recruitment consumes Relationship Capital to produce names, prospects, candidates and referral loops.

### Status
### Discovered.
### Not Approved.
### Not Implemented.


5.2 Career Capital

### Discovery status
Strongly indicated.

### Possible components

Market Natural.
Community membership.
Associations.
Centers of Influence.
Referral access.
Professional graph.
Social graph.
Trust capital.
Prospecting comfort.
P200 / Proyecto de Marketing.

### Relationship to Recruitment
Recruitment Intelligence consumes and activates Career Capital.

### Relationship to Productivity
Career Capital may be a leading indicator of future productivity.

### Status
### Discovered.
### Not Approved.
### Not Implemented.


5.3 Prospecting Intelligence

### Discovery status
Possible but not yet separate.

### Evidence
Training material treats prospecting as the central activity of the sales cycle, not only recruitment.

### Prospecting applies to

Client acquisition.
Advisor recruitment.
Referrals.
Centers of Influence.
Market Natural.

### Relationship to Recruitment
Recruitment may be one use case of a broader prospecting discipline.

### Status
DISCOVERED AS POSSIBLE HIGHER-ORDER CONCEPT.
### Do Not Create Domain Yet.


5.4 Recruitment remains valid.

### Important
The new discoveries do not eliminate Recruitment Intelligence.

They clarify that Recruitment Intelligence begins downstream of Relationship Capital and Market Natural.

### Recruitment is still needed to manage

Candidate funnel.
Interview stages.
Connection.
Signing.
Recruitment risk.
Source quality.
Recruitment network.
Recruitment decisions.


## 6. Recommended Next Step

## Recommended Next Step

Do not rewrite PAQ-02.

Create a PAQ-02 delta revision note or incorporate this addendum into PAQ-02 as an official addendum.

### Then perform a focused architecture review titled

Career Capital and Relationship Capital Boundary Review

### Purpose
### Determine whether Career Capital should be

1. A concept inside Shared Commercial Model.
2. A subdomain of Relationship Intelligence.
3. A dependency consumed by Recruitment Intelligence.
4. A future independent domain.

Do not implement.

Do not create schemas.

Do not create engines.

### Immediate required update to Recruitment Domain Model

### Change the root chain from

Name
Prospect
Candidate

### To

Relationship Capital
Market Natural
Person
Name
Prospect
Candidate

### Final addendum verdict

PAQ-02 remains valid as an ARCHITECTURE CANDIDATE.

However, it must be amended before Architecture Lock.

### The major correction is

Recruitment does not begin with names.

Recruitment begins with relationship capital.

### The official domain interpretation should become

Recruitment Intelligence converts relationship capital into candidate flow, candidate flow into advisor creation, and advisor creation into future Partner capacity.



===== PAQ-03-CAREER-CAPITAL-RELATIONSHIP-CAPITAL-BOUNDARY-REVIEW.md =====

# PAQ-03 Career Capital Relationship Capital Boundary Review

## Repository References

- [FORGE_MASTER_BUILD_TREE.md](FORGE_MASTER_BUILD_TREE.md)
- [AGENTS.md](AGENTS.md)
- [FORGE_CONSTITUTION_V3.md](FORGE_CONSTITUTION_V3.md)
- [FORGE_FOUNDATION_LOCK.md](FORGE_FOUNDATION_LOCK.md)

---

### Paq-03 Career Capital / Relationship Capital Boundary Review

### Mode
Principal Domain Architect

### Scope
Architecture boundary review only.

This document does not create code.
This document does not create engines.
This document does not create schemas.
This document does not modify UI.
This document does not commit changes.

### Input context

Foundation Lock is approved.
Recruitment Intelligence, codename Andrey Garcia, is ARCHITECTURE CANDIDATE.
Relationship Capital, Career Capital and Prospecting Intelligence are DISCOVERED only.

### Purpose
Determine what Relationship Capital, Career Capital and Prospecting Intelligence really are, where they live, who consumes them, who owns them, and whether they are domains, subdomains, capabilities, assets, evidence, interpretations or transversal concepts.


## 1. Executive Summary

### What we discovered

Recruitment Intelligence does not begin at the name.

The official training material shows that before a name appears there is a deeper commercial layer:

Relationships.
Communities.
Groups.
Market Natural.
Centers of Influence.
Referrals.
Trust.
Social access.
Professional access.
People who know people.

### The root discovery is this

Recruitment consumes relationship access.
Sales prospecting consumes relationship access.
Referral generation consumes relationship access.
Productivity depends partly on the advisor's ability to activate relationship access.
Partner growth depends partly on the Partner's ability to create advisors who can activate relationship access.

### The problem this PAQ is solving

PAQ-02 made Recruitment Intelligence an ARCHITECTURE CANDIDATE, but the ES training documents showed that the model still began too late.

### If Forge models recruitment as

Name
Prospect
Candidate

### then Forge misses the real upstream asset

Relationship Capital.

### Why this PAQ exists

Forge needs to prevent Recruitment Intelligence from incorrectly owning everything upstream.

Recruitment should not own all relationships, all communities, all Market Natural, all centers of influence, all referrals, all trust, or all social graph.

Recruitment should consume, activate and interpret part of that capital for recruiting purposes.

The deeper layer must be clarified before Recruitment Intelligence becomes ARCHITECTURE LOCK.

### Core conclusion

Relationship Capital is real.
Career Capital is real.
Recruitment consumes Relationship Capital.
Sales Prospecting consumes Relationship Capital.
Relationship Capital is shared between advisors, managers and Partners.
P200 is evidence of relationship capital.
PM is a network-expansion pattern.
CI is a trust and access amplifier.
The root cause underneath recruiting is the capacity to create, maintain and expand relationships.
The advisor-as-franchise metaphor is useful as a product and manager mental model, but not yet a constitutional principle.

### Final decision

### Relationship Capital
APPROVED as a transversal concept and shared asset model.
Not approved as an independent domain yet.

### Career Capital
DISCOVERED, strong candidate concept.
Not approved as a domain yet.

### Trust Transfer Principle
APPROVED as architecture principle candidate.
Not constitutional yet.

### Franchise Principle
DISCOVERED as useful model mental.
Not approved as formal principle.


## 2. Relationship Capital Review

### What Relationship Capital is

Relationship Capital is the durable commercial value created by a person's access to other people, groups, communities, trust paths and referral networks.

It is the usable relationship surface from which opportunities can emerge.

It exists before a specific sales opportunity, recruitment candidate or policy.

### It can be activated for

Recruitment.
Sales prospecting.
Referrals.
Centers of Influence.
Community development.
Partner development.
Advisor productivity.

### What Relationship Capital is not

It is not a contact list.
It is not a CRM record.
It is not only P200.
It is not only referrals.
It is not only client relationships.
It is not a compensation metric.
It is not proof of production.
It is not proof of sales skill.
It is not owned by Recruitment Intelligence alone.
It is not Forge Core as a domain.

### What Relationship Capital contains

Family.
Friends.
Colleagues.
Clients.
Ex-clients.
Communities.
Clubs.
Associations.
Schools.
Professional groups.
Social groups.
Religious or civic groups.
Centers of Influence.
Natural market contacts.
Referral paths.
Indirect access.
People who recognize the advisor.
People who trust the advisor.
People who trust someone who trusts the advisor.
Objects or situations that reveal people.

Is it an asset?

Yes.

Relationship Capital is best understood as a commercial asset.

It can increase, decay, be activated, be neglected, be transferred partially through trust, and produce opportunities.

Is it an entity?

Not as a single entity.

It is an aggregate concept composed from CommercialPerson, CommercialRelationship, CommercialAccount, CommercialAttribution, EvidenceRecord and snapshots.

Is it a capability?

Partly.

The existence of a network is an asset.
The ability to activate it is a capability.

### These must be separated

Relationship Capital = what relationship access exists.
Relationship Activation Capability = how well the advisor/Partner uses it.

Is it a network?

Yes, but not only a network.

The graph matters, but quality, trust, familiarity, permission, influence and actionability matter too.

Is it a domain?

Not yet.

It is approved as a transversal concept.
It may later justify a formal domain or subdomain, but this PAQ should not create one.

Is it Forge Core?

No.

Forge Core should provide the primitives needed to represent it:

CommercialPerson.
CommercialRelationship.
CommercialAccount.
CommercialAttribution.
CommercialAssignment.
EvidenceRecord.
ProvenanceRecord.
PeriodSnapshot.

Is it Shared Commercial Model?

Partly yes.

The primitives live in Shared Commercial Model.
The interpretation "Relationship Capital" should not be hardcoded as a Core primitive until its ownership is ratified.

Is it a transversal concept?

Yes.

It is consumed by Recruitment Intelligence, Sales Prospecting, Relationship Intelligence, Revenue Intelligence, Partner Intelligence, Productivity Intelligence and Business Planning.


## 3. Career Capital Review

### What Career Capital is

Career Capital is the set of assets, capabilities and credibility that make a person commercially viable as an advisor, Partner or commercial leader.

It includes relationship capital, but is broader.

### Relationship Capital answers

Who can this person reach, through what trust paths, and with what relationship access?

### Career Capital answers

What commercial assets and capabilities does this person bring into the career, and how likely are they to convert those assets into sustained productivity?

Is Career Capital different from Relationship Capital?

Yes.

Relationship Capital is one component of Career Capital.

### Career Capital may include

Market Natural.
P200 / Proyecto de Marketing.
Access to groups.
Ability to prospect.
Confidence to contact.
Trustworthiness.
Credibility.
Professional history.
Community membership.
Centers of Influence.
Referral access.
Sales maturity.
Discipline.
Coachability.
Communication capability.
Observed execution behavior.
Market familiarity.
Need-segmentation awareness.

### What belongs to Career Capital

Market Natural.
Community access.
Professional graph.
Social graph.
Relationship Capital.
Referral habits.
Centers of Influence.
P200 completion quality.
Ability to ask for referrals.
Ability to activate names.
Prospecting comfort.
Credibility in a market.
Commercial confidence.
Relevant career history.
Execution consistency when measured by Mick.

### What does not belong to Career Capital

Paid commissions.
Official compensation.
TA qualification.
Contest results.
Policy production as a raw fact.
Career stage as formal status.
Rule Pack compensation formulas.
Manager compensation.
Product knowledge by itself unless it affects commercial viability.

Is Career Capital an asset?

Yes.

It is an aggregate commercial asset.

Is it a score?

Not fundamentally.

It may produce scores or snapshots later, but reducing Career Capital to one score would be dangerous.

Is it a snapshot?

### It can produce snapshots

Initial Career Capital Snapshot.
Market Natural Snapshot.
Relationship Activation Snapshot.
Prospecting Capacity Snapshot.

But Career Capital itself is broader than a snapshot.

Is it a capability?

Partly.

It includes both assets and capabilities.

### Examples

### Asset
Existing social/professional network.

### Capability
Ability to activate that network.

Is it an interpretation?

Yes.

Career Capital is an interpretation over relationships, evidence, behavior, history and market access.

Is it a domain?

Not yet.

### Decision
Career Capital remains DISCOVERED.

It should not become a domain until Forge determines whether it belongs under Relationship Intelligence, Recruitment Intelligence, Advisor Experience, Career Intelligence or Shared Commercial Model as a cross-domain concept.


## 4. Boundary Analysis

4.1 Relationship Capital

### Purpose
Represent commercial value embedded in a person's relationships, access, trust paths and networks.

### Ownership
Transversal concept.
Underlying primitives owned by Shared Commercial Model.
Interpretations may be owned by consuming domains.

### Inputs
CommercialPerson.
CommercialRelationship.
CommercialAccount.
Relationship history.
Referral paths.
Community memberships.
CI relationships.
Evidence.
Provenance.

### Outputs
Relationship access context.
Trust path.
Referral potential.
Network quality.
Activation risk.

### Consumers
Recruitment Intelligence.
Sales Prospecting.
Relationship Intelligence.
Revenue Intelligence.
Partner Intelligence.
Productivity Intelligence.
Business Planning.


4.2 Career Capital

### Purpose
Represent a person's commercial viability and career-building assets.

### Ownership
DISCOVERED. No owner approved yet.

### Inputs
Relationship Capital.
Market Natural.
P200.
Prospecting activity.
Centers of Influence.
Referral capability.
Commercial history.
Credibility signals.
Mick behavior signals.

### Outputs
Career-capacity interpretation.
Prospecting capacity.
Market access risk.
Development priority.
Future productivity signal.

### Consumers
Recruitment Intelligence.
Career Intelligence.
Partner Intelligence.
Productivity Intelligence.
Business Planning.
Advisor Experience.


4.3 Recruitment Intelligence

### Purpose
Convert relationship and market access into candidate flow and future advisor capacity.

### Ownership
Recruitment funnel, recruitment source quality, recruitment stage movement, recruitment risk.

### Inputs
Relationship Capital.
Career Capital indicators.
P200 evidence.
PM referrals.
CI access.
Recruitment events.
Partner assignments.
Rule Pack targets.

### Outputs
Candidate pipeline.
Source quality.
Recruitment risks.
Funnel conversion.
Recruitment forecast.
Network expansion interpretation.

### Consumers
Partner Intelligence.
Forecast Intelligence.
Business Planning.
Productivity Intelligence.
Precontract Intelligence.


4.4 Sales Prospecting

### Purpose
Convert relationship and market access into client/prospect opportunities.

### Ownership
Not defined in this PAQ.
Likely belongs to Revenue Generation / Sales Prospecting domain already present in Forge.

### Inputs
Relationship Capital.
Market Natural.
Referrals.
CI.
Need segmentation.
Life events.
Relationship Intelligence.

### Outputs
Sales prospects.
Appointments.
Revenue opportunities.
Referral opportunities.

### Consumers
Revenue Intelligence.
Relationship Intelligence.
Business Planning.
Mick.


4.5 Partner Intelligence

### Purpose
Evaluate whether a Partner is creating, developing and scaling productive advisor units.

### Ownership
Partner-level interpretation and coaching context.

### Inputs
Recruitment pipeline.
Career Capital signals of candidates/advisors.
Relationship Capital activation.
Productivity.
Development.
Compensation outcomes.
Manager/Partner assignments.

### Outputs
Partner development risk.
Future unit capacity.
Coaching decisions.
Recruitment gap interpretation.
Development priority.

### Consumers
Manager Intelligence.
Business Planning.
Forecast Intelligence.
Compensation Intelligence.


4.6 Duplications identified

### Potential duplication
Recruitment Source vs Relationship Source.

### Resolution
RecruitmentSource is recruitment-context label.
CommercialRelationship is underlying relationship fact.

### Potential duplication
P200 vs Relationship Capital.

### Resolution
P200 is evidence/snapshot of relationship capital, not the capital itself.

### Potential duplication
PM as source vs PM as network pattern.

### Resolution
PM source label is local to Recruitment.
Magic Question pattern is a cross-context network expansion pattern.

### Potential duplication
Career Capital vs Productivity.

### Resolution
Career Capital is upstream capacity.
Productivity is downstream performance.


4.7 Conflicts identified

### Conflict
Recruitment may try to own all relationship data.

### Resolution
Recruitment consumes relationship data; Shared Commercial Model holds primitives.

### Conflict
Career Capital may become a vague score.

### Resolution
Keep it as interpreted aggregate until components and owners are clear.

### Conflict
Trust transfer may be treated as guaranteed quality.

### Resolution
Trust transfer increases probability/attention/confidence; it does not guarantee conversion.


## 5. P200 Analysis

### P200 is

### A list
Yes, operationally.

### An activity
Completing or updating P200 is an activity.

### Evidence
Yes. It is evidence of Market Natural and relationship inventory.

### A snapshot
Yes. At a point in time, it shows the state of a person's relationship inventory.

### An asset
Not directly. The relationships represented are the asset. The P200 is an artifact that evidences the asset.

### A score
No. It may contribute to a score or quality interpretation, but is not a score.

### What P200 measures

Relationship inventory.
Known people.
Market Natural breadth.
Initial prospecting surface.
Ability or willingness to list contacts.
Possible social/professional reach.

### What P200 predicts

Potential prospecting capacity.
Potential referral surface.
Risk of running out of people to contact.
Potential early activity base.
Potential friction in recruitment or sales.

### What P200 does not predict

It does not guarantee production.
It does not guarantee conversion.
It does not guarantee advisor quality.
It does not guarantee willingness to call.
It does not guarantee trust.
It does not guarantee sales skill.

Who should own P200?

### Recommended
Shared Commercial Model owns the underlying people/relationship primitives and evidence.

Career Capital, if later approved, should own interpretation of P200 as market/career asset.

Recruitment Intelligence consumes P200 for recruitment capacity and candidate evaluation.

Sales Prospecting consumes P200 for client prospecting capacity.

Mick consumes P200 activation behavior.

### Decision
P200 should not be owned exclusively by Recruitment.

### Best classification
P200 is a Rule Pack / training artifact that captures Market Natural evidence.
It should produce snapshots and be consumed by Recruitment, Sales Prospecting, Business Planning and Productivity/Partner interpretations.


## 6. Magic Question Analysis

### Recruitment Magic Question

"A quien invitarias a una entrevista como esta?"

### Sales equivalent

"A quien le serviria lo mismo que vimos hoy?"

### What they have in common

Both convert an interaction into network expansion.
Both use trust and context to generate new names.
Both depend on the current person's relationship graph.
Both work better when the current person trusts the advisor/Partner.
Both create indirect access.
Both can produce compounding growth.

Is PM a source?

Yes, in recruitment reporting.

But "PM" as source is only one local label.

Is PM a pattern?

Yes.

It is a reusable referral-generation pattern.

Is PM a technique?

Yes.

It is a conversation/prospecting technique.

Is PM a motor of expansion?

Yes.

It is a network expansion mechanism.

Does PM belong to Recruitment?

Recruitment owns PM use for recruiting candidates.

Does PM belong to Sales?

Sales Prospecting owns analogous referral requests for client prospects.

Does PM belong to a higher layer?

Yes, conceptually.

The higher layer is Relationship Capital activation or Prospecting pattern.

### Decision
Do not model Magic Question only as RecruitmentSource.

### Model it as

Local source label in Recruitment.
Referral-generation event.
Network-expansion pattern.
Relationship activation technique.


## 7. Center of Influence Review

Is CI a source?

Yes, operationally.

CI can be a recruitment source or sales prospecting source.

Is CI a person?

Usually yes.

A CI is generally a CommercialPerson with influence over a group or network.

Is CI a node?

Yes.

CI is a high-leverage node in a relationship graph.

Is CI a capacity?

Partly.

Having a CI relationship is an asset.
Cultivating and activating a CI is a capability.

Is CI Relationship Capital?

Yes.

CI is part of Relationship Capital because it represents trusted access to other people.

Is CI Career Capital?

Yes, when attached to an advisor or candidate as part of their career-building commercial asset.

### What decisions CI enables

Which influence relationships to cultivate.
Which group to access through trusted introduction.
Which CI is producing quality referrals.
Which CI relationship is stale.
Which Partner/advisor has strong network leverage.
Which CI can help rebuild a weak funnel.

### Architectural decision

CI should be modeled as a relationship/influence role over CommercialPerson and CommercialRelationship, not as a simple source string.


## 8. Trust Transfer Principle Review

### Hypothesis
Higher quality opportunities arise through transfer of trust.

### Evidence from training material

Referrals matter because the referred person gives attention due to association.
The value of the advisor's service is pre-established by the referring person.
The referred person has initial trust because the referrer trusts the advisor.
Centers of Influence create access through respect and recommendation.
Market Natural begins with people who recognize the advisor.

### RDA

High trust transfer when the referring advisor is credible.
Risk: advisor may refer weak-fit names.

### PM

Medium to high trust transfer depending on the originating candidate and relationship depth.
Risk: may generate volume without quality.

### CI

High trust transfer when CI is respected and active.
Risk: CI can decay or stop referring.

### Client referrals

High trust transfer when client is satisfied and relationship is strong.
Risk: client may not know who is a good fit.

### Market Natural

Variable trust transfer.
Recognition and familiarity help, but do not guarantee need or willingness.

### FF

Low trust transfer.
May still work through skill, timing, need or volume, but starts with lower inherited confidence.

Should Trust Transfer Principle become constitutional?

Not yet.

It has enough evidence to become an architecture principle candidate, but not constitutional doctrine.

### Reason

Trust transfer is powerful but not absolute.
High trust can still produce low quality.
Cold sources can still produce success.
Relationship access can create opportunity but not guarantee action.

### Recommended status
APPROVED as architecture principle candidate.
Not constitutional.

### Principle statement candidate

Forge should identify and preserve the trust path behind opportunities because trust transfer affects attention, conversion probability, relationship quality and recommended next action.


## 9. Franchise Principle Review

### Statement
An advisor is a franchise.
The Partner's job is to open franchises.

Is it a useful metaphor?

Yes.

It explains that each advisor is not merely an employee or producer.
Each advisor can be viewed as an economic unit with its own market, activity, relationships, productivity and growth potential.

Does it explain productivity?

Partly.

It helps explain that productivity depends on the advisor's ability to activate their own market, relationships, habits and sales process.

Does it explain development?

Yes.

If an advisor is a franchise-like unit, development is not generic training.
Development is the process of making that unit commercially viable.

Does it explain promotion?

Partly.

Promotion may be understood as a shift from operating one unit to developing multiple units.

Does it explain Partner Intelligence?

Yes, as a model mental.

### Partner Intelligence can ask

Is this Partner opening viable advisor units?
Are those units developing?
Are they productive?
Are they expanding their own relationship capital?
Are they self-sustaining?

Should it become a principle?

Not yet.

It is too metaphorical for constitutional or domain lock.

### It should remain a model mental until validated against

Compensation rules.
Development outcomes.
Productivity patterns.
Advisor retention.
Promotion paths.
Manager/Partner economics.

### Recommended status
### Discovered.

### Best use
Product and management reasoning, not Core architecture.


## 10. Shared Commercial Model Impact

10.1 CommercialPerson

### Should live here

### Every person in Relationship Capital
Family member.
Friend.
Client.
Ex-client.
Candidate.
Advisor.
Partner.
CI.
Referrer.
Prospect.

### Should not live here

Relationship Capital score.
Career Capital interpretation.
Recruitment funnel stage.
Trust transfer score as hardcoded field.


10.2 CommercialRelationship

### Should live here

### Relationships between people

Family.
Friend.
Colleague.
Client.
Ex-client.
Referral.
CI access.
Professional association.
Community membership.
Introduced by.
Knows.
Recognizes.
Referred by.

### Should not live here

Recruitment-specific stage logic.
Compensation credit without attribution.
Forecasts.
Rule Pack thresholds.


10.3 CommercialAssignment

### Should live here

### Time-bounded responsibility

Partner responsible for candidate pipeline.
Manager responsible for advisor.
Office assignment.
Recruitment ownership assignment.

### Should not live here

Referral origin.
Trust transfer.
CI influence.
Source quality.


10.4 CommercialAttribution

### Should live here

### Credit/origin relationships

Who referred.
Who connected.
Who introduced.
Who developed.
Who created network access.
Who receives credit under a Rule Pack.

### Should not live here

Current servicing.
Relationship itself without credit.
Manager responsibility.
Payment unless Compensation says so.


10.5 CommercialAccount

### Should live here

### Groups or accounts that organize relationship access

Family.
Household.
Business.
Community organization.
Professional group.
Affinity group.

### Should not live here

Recruitment funnel state.
Advisor productivity.
Career Capital interpretation.


10.6 Concepts that should live in Shared Commercial Model

CommercialPerson.
CommercialRelationship.
CommercialAccount.

PeriodSnapshot.

### Possible future shared concepts

RelationshipGroup.
CommunityMembership.
InfluenceRole.
ReferralRelationship.
