These should be evaluated carefully before implementation.


10.7 Concepts that should not live in Shared Commercial Model

Recruitment risk.
Source quality interpretation.
Career Capital score.
Recruitment funnel stage.
Business planning action.
Forecasted pipeline shortage.
Partner coaching recommendation.
Compensation result.
Rule Pack-specific source thresholds.


## 11. Red Team Review

### Scenario 1
Person with large network and zero production.

### Failure
Relationship Capital alone does not equal productivity.

### Limit
Relationship Capital must be separated from activation capability, sales skill and behavior.

### Guardrail
Do not treat network size as success.


### Scenario 2
Person with small network and high production.

### Failure
Relationship Capital model may under-value skill, niche, discipline or high-quality small networks.

### Limit
Relationship quality and activation matter more than raw size.

### Guardrail
Measure conversion and activity, not only graph size.


### Scenario 3
PM generates volume but not quality.

### Failure
Magic Question as source count becomes vanity metric.

### Limit
PM must be evaluated by downstream conversion and referral-chain quality.

### Guardrail
PM count is not PM value.


### Scenario 4
CI stops referring.

### Failure
CI as static asset overstates current value.

### Limit
Relationship Capital decays.

### Guardrail
Track relationship freshness, activity and recent referral output.


### Scenario 5
P200 complete but never activated.

### Failure
P200 as asset or score becomes misleading.

### Limit
P200 is evidence, not execution.

### Guardrail
Separate P200 completion from P200 activation.


### Scenario 6
Advisor successful without Market Natural.

### Failure
Career Capital model may overemphasize Market Natural.

### Limit
Some advisors can build through cold prospecting, digital channels, niche expertise, institutional access or strong sales skill.

### Guardrail
Market Natural is a leading indicator, not a universal requirement.


### Scenario 7
Recruitment successful without Relationship Capital.

### Failure
Relationship Capital may be too broad or under-detected.

### Limit
Some recruitment can come from cold campaigns, brand, job boards or institutional pipelines.

### Guardrail
Do not reject FF or non-relationship sources. Treat them as lower trust transfer, not invalid.


### Scenario 8
High production with few relationships.

### Failure
Relationship count may not explain quality of relationship, account size, niche, or high-value market access.

### Limit
CommercialAccount quality and opportunity value matter.

### Guardrail
Measure relationship quality and economic conversion, not only number of relationships.


### Red Team conclusion

Relationship Capital is real but dangerous if reduced to size.
Career Capital is real but dangerous if reduced to one score.
Trust Transfer is real but not deterministic.
Franchise Principle is useful but too metaphorical for lock.


## 12. Architecture Decision

### Relationship Capital
APPROVED

### Decision meaning
Approved as a transversal architecture concept and shared commercial asset model.

### Not approved as
Independent domain.
Implementation.
Schema.
Score.

### Why
Evidence is strong across ES training material and Recruitment PAQs.
It explains the upstream layer before names, prospects and candidates.
It is required by Recruitment, Sales Prospecting, Relationship Intelligence and Partner Intelligence.


### Career Capital
DISCOVERED

### Decision meaning
Recognized as real and important, but not yet approved as a formal domain or locked model.

### Why
It is broader than Relationship Capital and likely includes behavior, credibility, market access, prospecting ability and commercial skill.
Ownership is still unclear.
It may overlap with Career Intelligence, Mick, Advisor Experience, Recruitment and Partner Intelligence.


### Trust Transfer Principle
APPROVED

### Decision meaning
Approved as architecture principle candidate for future domain design.

### Not approved as
Constitutional principle.
Rule.
Formula.
Guarantee.

### Why
Training material gives strong evidence that referrals and CI improve attention, perceived value and initial trust.
However, trust transfer does not guarantee conversion or quality.


### Franchise Principle
DISCOVERED

### Decision meaning
Useful model mental for Partner Intelligence and development conversations.

### Not approved as
Constitutional principle.
Domain.
Core model.

### Why
It explains advisor economic units and Partner leverage, but remains metaphorical and needs validation against productivity, development, retention and compensation evidence.


## 13. Recommended Next Step

## Recommended Next Step
Recruitment Hardening.

### Why

Recruitment Intelligence is already ARCHITECTURE CANDIDATE.
PAQ-02 now has a clear addendum and this PAQ clarifies the upstream boundary.
The next useful work is not to open Partner, Productivity, Forecast or Business Planning yet.
The next useful work is to harden Recruitment with the corrected root:

Relationship Capital
Market Natural
Person
Name
Prospect
Candidate

### Recruitment Hardening should update

Recruitment boundary.
P200 as relationship capital evidence.
PM as network expansion.
CI as influence node.
Recruitment Risk as first-class.
Trust Transfer as source quality factor.
Forecast guardrails for future talent shortage.
Relationship Capital dependency.

### Why not Partner Intelligence next

Partner Intelligence depends on reliable recruitment semantics.

### Why not Productivity Intelligence next

Productivity depends on recruitment and development input quality.

### Why not Forecast Intelligence next

Forecast needs stable recruitment metrics and risks first.

### Why not Business Planning next

Business Planning needs stable goal, forecast, gap and action inputs from Recruitment first.


## 14. Final Verdict

### Final finding

The true root layer is not Recruitment.

The true root layer is the capacity to create, maintain and expand relationships.

Recruitment is one way of activating that capacity.

Sales prospecting is another.

Partner growth depends on creating advisors who can activate that capacity repeatedly.

### Official corrected causal root

Relationship Capital
Career Capital
Prospecting Activation
Names
Prospects
Candidates
Connected
Signed
Developed
Productive
Compensated

Recruitment Intelligence remains valid.

But Recruitment Intelligence must not own the relationship layer.

It consumes it.
It activates it.
It expands it.
It interprets it for recruiting decisions.

Relationship Capital should be accepted as an approved transversal architecture concept.

Career Capital should remain discovered until ownership is clarified.

Trust Transfer should be accepted as an approved architecture principle candidate.

Franchise Principle should remain discovered as a useful model mental.

### Recommended project direction

Proceed to Recruitment Hardening before opening Partner Intelligence, Productivity Intelligence, Forecast Intelligence or Business Planning Intelligence.

### Reason

The Intelligence Phase should start with a hardened recruitment root because future Partner growth depends on whether Forge can correctly explain how relationship capital becomes advisor capacity.



===== PAQ-04-P200-MARKET-NATURAL-DISCOVERY-REVIEW.md =====

# PAQ-04 P200 Market Natural Discovery Review

## Repository References

- [FORGE_MASTER_BUILD_TREE.md](FORGE_MASTER_BUILD_TREE.md)
- [AGENTS.md](AGENTS.md)
- [FORGE_CONSTITUTION_V3.md](FORGE_CONSTITUTION_V3.md)
- [FORGE_FOUNDATION_LOCK.md](FORGE_FOUNDATION_LOCK.md)

---


### Mode
Principal Domain Architect

### Scope
Architecture correction and boundary review only.

This document does not create code.
This document does not create engines.
This document does not create schemas.
This document does not modify UI.
This document does not commit changes.

### Architecture correction

P200 does not belong to Recruitment Intelligence.
P200 is not a Recruitment Artifact.
P200 is not a prospect list.

P200 is a Market Natural Discovery Artifact.

Recruitment Intelligence consumes P200.
Sales Prospecting consumes P200.
Partner Intelligence consumes P200.
Business Planning consumes P200.

### Corrected causal flow

Relationship Capital
Market Natural
P200 Evidence
Recruitment
Sales Prospecting


## 1. Executive Summary

### The critical correction is valid

P200 should not be owned by Recruitment Intelligence.

P200 is not primarily a recruitment tool.

P200 is an artifact used to discover and externalize Market Natural.

Its main purpose is not to create candidates.

Its main purpose is to reveal the advisor's or candidate's relationship inventory and market access surface.

### P200 helps Forge see

Relationship inventory.
Market Natural.
Relationship clusters.
Community access.
Market concentration.
Potential relationship activation surface.
Potential prospecting capacity.
Potential referral capacity.
Potential recruiting capacity.

Recruitment may use P200 to identify candidate capacity and future recruiting surfaces.

Sales Prospecting may use P200 to identify client/prospect opportunities.

Partner Intelligence may use P200 to evaluate whether a potential or new advisor has enough market surface to become a viable economic unit.

Business Planning may use P200 to estimate whether activity goals have enough relationship surface behind them.

But P200 itself is not Recruitment.

Market Natural is the discovered relationship field.
P200 is evidence of that field.
Relationship Capital is the broader asset.
Career Capital is the broader career viability interpretation.

### Final summary

Market Natural should be APPROVED as a distinct conceptual layer inside Relationship Capital.

P200 should be APPROVED as Market Natural evidence and snapshot artifact.

P200 should be explicitly removed from Recruitment ownership.


## 2. Market Natural Definition

### What Market Natural really is

Market Natural is the set of people, groups, communities and relationship clusters that a person can naturally identify, access, recognize or be recognized by at the beginning of a commercial career or prospecting process.

It is the person's natural reachable market.

It includes people with whom there is some prior familiarity, shared context, common group, relational path, community membership, professional adjacency or recognition.

Market Natural exists before the person becomes a candidate in recruitment, before a prospect becomes a client, and before any sale occurs.

Market Natural is not a list.

A list can represent it.
P200 can reveal it.
But the Market Natural itself is the underlying commercial/social field.

### Market Natural contains

Family.
Friends.
Former classmates.
Current classmates.
Former coworkers.
Current coworkers.
Neighbors.
Community members.
Club members.
Service providers.
Business owners frequented by the person.
Professional groups.
School communities.
Parent groups.
Religious or civic communities.
Sports or hobby communities.
People known through spouse/partner.
People known through clients.
People known through advisors.
People reachable through centers of influence.

### What Market Natural is not

It is not Recruitment.
It is not a CRM.
It is not a P200.
It is not a candidate list.
It is not a prospect list.
It is not proof of production.
It is not proof of sales ability.
It is not proof of trust.
It is not proof of conversion.
It is not compensation.
It is not a Rule Pack result.

Is Market Natural a concept?

Yes.

It is a business concept recognized by training material and operational artifacts.

Is Market Natural an asset?

Yes, but with nuance.

The relationship access inside Market Natural is an asset.
The named inventory is evidence of the asset.

Is Market Natural a capability?

Not directly.

Market Natural is mostly an asset/surface.

The capability is the ability to activate Market Natural.

Is Market Natural evidence?

No.

Market Natural itself is not evidence.
P200 and Proyecto de Marketing are evidence of Market Natural.

Is Market Natural a snapshot?

No.

Market Natural can be snapshotted.
It is not itself a snapshot.

Is Market Natural an interpretation?

Partly.

The raw relationships are facts.
The interpretation that these relationships form a usable Market Natural is an interpretation.

Is Market Natural a domain?

Not yet.

Market Natural should not become a standalone domain at this stage.

Is Market Natural a subdomain?

Possibly later under Relationship Capital, Career Capital, Sales Prospecting or Advisor Development.

### Current decision
Treat Market Natural as a distinct conceptual layer and interpreted asset surface inside Relationship Capital.


## 3. Relationship Capital Boundary

Relationship Capital is broader than Market Natural.

### Relationship Capital means

The durable commercial value embedded in a person's relationships, trust paths, referral paths, community access, influence access and network position.

Market Natural is one expression of Relationship Capital.

### Relationship Capital includes

Market Natural.
Existing clients.
Former clients.
Referral relationships.
Centers of Influence.
Professional graph.
Social graph.
Trust paths.
Community memberships.
Influence nodes.
Indirect access.
Relationship quality.
Relationship freshness.

### Market Natural differs from Relationship Capital because

Market Natural is the naturally identifiable and accessible starting market.
Relationship Capital is the broader asset that includes all relationship value, including developed client relationships, referral paths, influence relationships and network trust over time.

Can Relationship Capital exist without Market Natural?

Yes.

### Examples

An advisor builds strong client relationships over time despite a weak initial natural market.
A person has one powerful CI but no broad natural market.
A professional has deep institutional access but little personal market.
A digital prospecting system produces relationships not originally from Market Natural.

Can Market Natural exist without Relationship Capital?

Only superficially.

If Market Natural is merely a list of names with no familiarity, access, trust, recognition or relationship path, then it is not meaningful Market Natural.

A weak or low-quality Market Natural can exist as shallow relationship inventory, but usable Market Natural requires at least minimal Relationship Capital.

### Boundary decision

Market Natural is a subset or expression of Relationship Capital, not an equivalent term.


## 4. Career Capital Boundary

Career Capital is broader than both Relationship Capital and Market Natural.

### Career Capital means

The combined commercial assets, capabilities, credibility and behaviors that make a person viable in an advisor career or commercial leadership path.

### Career Capital may include

Relationship Capital.
Market Natural.
P200 evidence.
Credibility.
Commercial confidence.
Ability to prospect.
Ability to ask for referrals.
Communication skill.
Coachability.
Discipline.
Market understanding.
Professional background.
Community reputation.
Centers of Influence.
Sales maturity.
Execution behavior.

### How Market Natural differs from Career Capital

### Market Natural answers
Who can this person naturally reach or identify?

### Career Capital answers
Can this person convert their assets, relationships, behavior and credibility into a sustainable career?

### How Relationship Capital differs from Career Capital

Relationship Capital is relationship access and trust value.

Career Capital includes Relationship Capital but adds personal capability, commercial maturity, execution discipline and career viability.

### Boundary decision

Career Capital should not own P200 directly at this stage.

Career Capital may consume P200/Market Natural interpretation as one component of broader career viability.


## 5. P200 Analysis

### What P200 is

P200 is a Market Natural Discovery Artifact.

It is a structured exercise to externalize the person's natural market.

### It is an artifact that reveals or attempts to reveal

Relationship inventory.
Recognized people.
Familiar people.
Relationship clusters.
Community access.
Market concentration.
Potential activation surface.

### What P200 is not

It is not Recruitment.
It is not a Recruitment Artifact.
It is not a prospect list.
It is not a candidate list.
It is not a guarantee of productivity.
It is not a guarantee of quality.
It is not a guarantee of trust.
It is not a metric of advisor success by itself.

Does P200 measure Market Natural or Relationship Capital?

P200 primarily measures or evidences Market Natural.

It indirectly evidences part of Relationship Capital.

### More precisely

P200 is evidence of declared Market Natural.
Declared Market Natural is a subset/expression of Relationship Capital.

What part is evidence?

The listed names.
Known relationship type.
Contactability.
Group membership.
Occupation.
Age or life stage if captured.
Time known.
Frequency of interaction.
Possibility of approach.
Potential for referrals.
Comments.
Source of the relationship.

What part is interpretation?

Market strength.
Relationship quality.
Activation potential.
Trust level.
Referral potential.
Market concentration.
Prospecting capacity.
Recruitment capacity.
Sales opportunity quality.
Career viability implication.

Is P200 a list?

Operationally yes.
Architecturally no.

It is not only a list.
It is evidence of a relationship inventory.

Is P200 an activity?

Completing P200 is an activity.
Updating P200 is an activity.
Reviewing P200 is an activity.
Activating names from P200 is an activity.

The artifact itself is not only an activity.

Is P200 evidence?

Yes.

It is evidence of declared Market Natural.

Is P200 a snapshot?

Yes, when captured at a point in time.

### Example
P200 Snapshot as of a date.

Is P200 an asset?

No.

The underlying Market Natural / Relationship Capital is the asset.
P200 is a representation of the asset.

Is P200 a score?

No.

It may contribute to interpretation, but it is not a score.

### What P200 predicts

Potential available people to contact.
Potential prospecting capacity.
Potential recruitment capacity.
Potential referral surface.
Potential market concentration.
Risk of market exhaustion.
Risk of weak relationship inventory.

### What P200 does not predict

Conversion.
Sales skill.
Trust depth.
Willingness to call.
Actual production.
Actual recruitment success.
Actual compensation.
Future productivity with certainty.

### Valid metrics

Declared relationship count.
Distinct relationship clusters.
Community/group count.
Contactability rate.
Relationship type distribution.
Time-known distribution.
Interaction-frequency distribution.
Approachability distribution.
Referral-potential distribution.
Market concentration by cluster.
Activation rate.
Contacted-from-P200 rate.
Appointment-from-P200 rate.
Referral-from-P200 rate.
Candidate-from-P200 rate.
Client-from-P200 rate.
Conversion by cluster.
Staleness / freshness of relationship inventory.

### Vanity metrics

Raw P200 count alone.
Percentage completion alone.
Number of names without contactability.
Number of names without relationship type.
Number of names without activation.
Number of clusters without conversion.
Referral potential declared but never tested.
Market Natural score without evidence.


## 6. Ownership Analysis

6.1 Shared Commercial Model

### Owns

CommercialPerson.
CommercialRelationship.
CommercialAccount.
CommercialAttribution.
CommercialAssignment.
EvidenceRecord.
ProvenanceRecord.
PeriodSnapshot.

### Should own

The universal primitives needed to represent people, groups, relationships, evidence and source provenance.

### Should not own

Market Natural interpretation.
Recruitment risk.
Sales prospecting decisions.
Partner coaching interpretation.
Business planning actions.


6.2 Market Natural

### Ownership status
No standalone domain approved.

### Recommended conceptual ownership
Transversal concept over Shared Commercial Model primitives.

### Interpretation owners

Recruitment interprets for candidate/recruiting capacity.
Sales Prospecting interprets for prospect/client capacity.
Partner Intelligence interprets for advisor unit viability.
Business Planning interprets for goal feasibility and activation surface.


6.3 P200

### Ownership
Not Recruitment.

### Recommended owner
Shared evidence layer for the artifact.

### Recommended interpretation
Market Natural Discovery Artifact.

### Consumers

Recruitment Intelligence.
Sales Prospecting.
Partner Intelligence.
Business Planning.
Career Capital interpretation if later approved.
Advisor Experience if used for baseline or setup.
Mick if tracking completion/activation behavior.


6.4 Recruitment Intelligence

### Consumes

P200 evidence.
Market Natural interpretation.
Relationship clusters.
Referral potential.
Community access.
Activation risk.

### Uses P200 to answer

Does this candidate/advisor have enough relationship surface for recruiting?
Which clusters might produce candidate names?
Which P200 contacts could become recruitment prospects?
Where is recruitment capacity weak?

### Does not own

P200.
Market Natural.
Relationship Capital.


6.5 Sales Prospecting

### Consumes

P200 evidence.
Market Natural.
Relationship clusters.
Community access.
Need segmentation.
Trust paths.

### Uses P200 to answer

Who can become a client prospect?
Which clusters can produce appointments?
Which relationships can generate referrals?
Which market segment is overrepresented?

### Does not own

P200 artifact as universal evidence.


6.6 Partner Intelligence

### Consumes

P200 evidence.
Market Natural strength.
Relationship cluster diversity.
Activation surface.
Recruitment outcomes.
Productivity outcomes.

### Uses P200 to answer

Is this advisor/candidate a viable economic unit?
Does this person have enough market surface to start?
Does the Partner's future unit have relationship capital?
Which advisors need development around activation?

### Does not own

Raw P200 artifact.
Recruitment candidate stages.
Sales prospecting pipeline.


6.7 Business Planning Intelligence

### Consumes

P200 evidence.
Market Natural interpretation.
Activation rates.
Source quality.
Recruitment funnel.
Sales prospecting funnel.
Mick behavior.

### Uses P200 to answer

Are goals feasible given available relationship surface?
Does the plan have enough names/relationships behind it?
What activation actions are required?
Which clusters should be activated first?

### Does not own

P200.
Relationship graph.
Recruitment metrics.
Sales prospecting metrics.


## 7. Red Team Review

### Hypothesis to destroy
"A complete P200 implies a strong Market Natural."

### Verdict
False.

A complete P200 may indicate effort, memory, compliance or administrative completion.

It does not automatically prove strong Market Natural.


7.1 Counterexample: 200 weak names

### Scenario
The person lists 200 names but has not spoken to most of them in years.

### Failure
Raw count looks strong, activation surface is weak.

### Conclusion
Completeness does not equal relationship strength.


7.2 Counterexample: 200 names without contactability

### Scenario
Names lack phone, channel, permission or context.

### Failure
Market cannot be activated.

### Conclusion
Contactability matters.


7.3 Counterexample: 200 names in one cluster

### Scenario
All names come from one school, one job or one family branch.

### Failure
Market concentration risk.

### Conclusion
Diversity of clusters matters.


7.4 Counterexample: high familiarity, low commercial fit

### Scenario
The person knows many people, but most lack need, income, seriousness or decision capacity.

### Failure
Relationship inventory is real but commercial opportunity is limited.

### Conclusion
Market Natural is not equivalent to qualified opportunity.


7.5 Counterexample: P200 completed by pressure

### Scenario
Candidate fills names mechanically to satisfy training requirement.

### Failure
Artifact exists but evidence quality is low.

### Conclusion
P200 requires confidence/provenance and validation.


7.6 Counterexample: small P200, strong Market Natural

### Scenario
Candidate lists only 80 names but each cluster is high-trust, active and referral-rich.

### Failure
Raw completion underestimates strength.

### Conclusion
Quality can outweigh quantity.


7.7 Counterexample: weak Market Natural, high cold-prospecting skill

### Scenario
Advisor has little natural market but excels in cold prospecting or digital acquisition.

### Failure
P200 underestimates career potential.

### Conclusion
Market Natural is one input, not the whole career model.


7.8 Counterexample: strong P200, no activation behavior

### Scenario
Advisor has a rich P200 but never contacts, asks, follows up or activates.

### Failure
Relationship asset remains dormant.

### Conclusion
Mick behavior and activation metrics are required.


7.9 False positives

Raw 200 names.
High completion percentage.
Many recognizable names.
Many family names.
Many social media contacts.
Many declared potential referrals.

### Why false
They may not convert into contact, appointment, referral, candidate, prospect, client or advisor.


7.10 False negatives

Small list with high trust.
Small professional niche.
One powerful CI.
Few but active community clusters.
Strong digital audience not represented in P200.
Institutional access not captured by personal names.

### Why false
P200 may miss non-traditional access or high-quality concentrated markets.


7.11 Errors if Forge confuses Relationship Capital, Market Natural and P200

### Error
Treating P200 as Relationship Capital.

### Consequence
Forge believes a list is the asset.

### Error
Treating Market Natural as Recruitment.

### Consequence
Recruitment incorrectly owns broader relationship/career surface.

### Error
Treating Relationship Capital as P200 count.

### Consequence
Trust, access, group structure and relationship quality disappear.

### Error
Treating P200 completion as career viability.

### Consequence
False positives in candidate/advisor assessment.

### Error
Treating no P200 as no market.

### Consequence
False negatives for people with non-traditional networks.


## 8. Architecture Recommendation

8.1 Market Natural status

### Decision
APPROVED as a distinct conceptual layer inside Relationship Capital.

### Not approved as
Standalone domain.
Implementation.
Schema.
Score.


8.2 P200 status

### Decision
APPROVED as Market Natural Discovery Artifact.

### Not approved as
Recruitment Artifact.
Prospect list.
Candidate list.
Score.
Guarantee.


8.3 Ownership recommendation

### Shared Commercial Model
Owns primitives and evidence structures.

### Market Natural
Conceptual layer over Relationship Capital.

### P200
Evidence/snapshot artifact for Market Natural.

### Recruitment
Consumes P200.

### Sales Prospecting
Consumes P200.

### Partner Intelligence
Consumes P200.

### Business Planning
Consumes P200.

### Mick
Consumes completion/activation behavior.


8.4 Foundation principles affected

### Capture Once
P200 should be captured once and reused by Recruitment, Sales Prospecting, Partner Intelligence and Business Planning.

### One Metric One Owner
P200 count, activation rate and interpretation metrics must have clear owners.

### Facts First
Listed names are evidence/facts only when provenance and confidence exist.
Market strength is interpretation.

### Rule Pack Separation
P200 format and required count may be SMNYL-specific.
Market Natural concept is broader.

### Forecasts Are Suggestions
P200 can support forecasts but cannot guarantee outcomes.

### Economic Clarity
P200 may inform future economic potential only with evidence, rules and confidence.

### Advisor First
P200 should help advisors understand and activate their market, not become paperwork.


8.5 Implications for Recruitment Intelligence

Recruitment Intelligence must remove ownership claim over P200.

### Recruitment should consume

P200 evidence.
Market Natural clusters.
Activation surface.
Referral potential.
Relationship concentration.

### Recruitment should interpret

Recruitment candidate potential.
Recruitment source opportunities.
Recruiting risk.
Potential candidate/referral paths.

### Recruitment should not interpret

Full Career Capital.
Full Relationship Capital.
Sales prospecting potential outside recruitment.
Official Partner economic value.


8.6 Implications for Business Planning Intelligence

Business Planning should use P200 to test feasibility of goals.

### Questions

Does the goal have enough relationship surface behind it?
Which cluster should be activated?
Is the plan relying on names that are not contactable?
Is market concentration creating risk?
Is the advisor's activity plan realistic given Market Natural?

Business Planning must not treat P200 as automatic capacity.


8.7 Implications for Partner Intelligence

Partner Intelligence should use P200 to understand whether a potential advisor unit has market surface.

### Questions

Does this advisor have a viable natural market?
Is the market concentrated or diversified?
Is the advisor activating it?
Does the Partner need to coach referral asking, CI development or market expansion?
Is the Partner opening viable units or just signing people?

Partner Intelligence must not equate complete P200 with future productivity.


## 9. Final Verdict

### Market Natural
APPROVED as distinct conceptual layer inside Relationship Capital.

### P200
APPROVED as Market Natural Discovery Artifact and evidence/snapshot of declared Market Natural.

### Relationship Capital
Remains broader than Market Natural.

### Career Capital
Consumes Market Natural as one component but remains broader and still not locked as a domain.

### Recruitment Intelligence
Consumes P200 but does not own it.

### Sales Prospecting
Consumes P200 but does not own it.

### Partner Intelligence
Consumes P200 as advisor-unit viability signal but does not own it.

### Business Planning
Consumes P200 for feasibility and activation planning but does not own it.

### Architecture correction
### PAQ-02 and PAQ-03 should be interpreted with this correction

P200 is not recruitment.
P200 is not a prospect list.
P200 is a Market Natural Discovery Artifact.

### Corrected model

Relationship Capital
Market Natural
P200 Evidence
Recruitment
Sales Prospecting

### Red Team conclusion

A complete P200 does not imply a strong Market Natural.

Strong Market Natural requires contactability, trust, relationship quality, cluster diversity, activation potential and downstream conversion.

### Final recommendation

Proceed to Recruitment Hardening only after updating its boundary:

Recruitment starts after Market Natural evidence is consumed and interpreted for recruitment purposes.

Recruitment does not own Market Natural.

Recruitment activates part of it.



===== PAQ-05-RELATIONSHIP-ACTIVATION-REVIEW.md =====

# PAQ-05 Relationship Activation Review

## Repository References

- [FORGE_MASTER_BUILD_TREE.md](FORGE_MASTER_BUILD_TREE.md)
- [AGENTS.md](AGENTS.md)
- [FORGE_CONSTITUTION_V3.md](FORGE_CONSTITUTION_V3.md)
- [FORGE_FOUNDATION_LOCK.md](FORGE_FOUNDATION_LOCK.md)

---


### Mode
Principal Domain Architect

### Scope
Architecture discovery and boundary review only.

This document does not create code.
This document does not create engines.
This document does not create schemas.
This document does not modify UI.
This document does not commit changes.

### Context

### PAQ-02 Recruitment Domain Model
ARCHITECTURE CANDIDATE

### PAQ-03 Boundary Review
LOCK

### PAQ-04 Market Natural Discovery Review
LOCK

### Approved discoveries

### Relationship Capital
APPROVED transversal concept.

### Market Natural
APPROVED conceptual layer.

### P200
APPROVED Market Natural Discovery Artifact.

### Trust Transfer
APPROVED architecture principle candidate.

### New hypothesis

Relationships do not produce results by themselves.
Relationship activation produces results.


## 1. Executive Summary

Relationship Activation is the missing layer between relationship potential and commercial outcome.

### Relationship Capital answers
What relationship access exists?

### Market Natural answers
Where is the natural reachable market?

### P200 answers
Can the market be seen and externalized?

### Relationship Activation answers
Is the relationship asset being used, contacted, converted, refreshed and expanded?

This PAQ exists because two people can have the same Relationship Capital, the same Market Natural and the same P200 evidence, but produce radically different outcomes.

The difference is not the asset.
The difference is activation.

### Example

### Person A
200 names.
0 calls.
0 Magic Questions.
0 appointments.
0 follow-up.
0 results.

### Person B
80 names.
20 calls.
10 Magic Questions.
8 appointments.
Repeated follow-up.
Higher productivity.

### The architecture problem

Forge must not confuse relationship inventory with relationship use.

Relationship Activation is the observable conversion of relationship access into commercial movement.

It is not a standalone domain at this stage.

It is an approved transversal capability and interpretation layer over relationship events, activity events and domain outcomes.

### It is consumed by

Recruitment Intelligence.
Sales Prospecting.
Relationship Intelligence.
Partner Intelligence.
Business Planning Intelligence.
Forecast Intelligence.
Mick.

It is not owned exclusively by Mick.

Mick owns behavior discipline and execution patterns.
Relationship Activation owns the commercial meaning of using relationship access.

### Final decision

### Relationship Activation
APPROVED as transversal capability and interpretation layer.

### Not approved as
Standalone domain.
Forge Core primitive.
Implementation.
Schema.
Engine.


## 2. Activation Definition

### Relationship Capital responds
What do I have?

### Market Natural responds
Where is it?

### P200 responds
Can I see it?

### Relationship Activation responds
Am I using it?
Am I contacting it?
Am I converting it?
Am I refreshing it?
Am I expanding it?
Am I transforming relationship potential into commercial movement?

### Precise definition

Relationship Activation is the set of actions, events and interpreted patterns through which a person uses existing or accessible relationships to create contact, appointments, referrals, introductions, interviews, opportunities, candidates, clients, or network expansion.

Relationship Activation is not the relationship itself.

It is the observable use of the relationship.

### Relationship Activation has four core dimensions

### Use
Was the relationship contacted or engaged?

### Conversion
Did the contact become an appointment, interview, referral, opportunity, candidate or client?

### Expansion
Did the relationship generate more relationships, names, introductions or referrals?

### Refresh
Was a stale or dormant relationship reconnected or revived?

### Activation can apply to

P200 names.
Market Natural clusters.
Centers of Influence.
Clients.
Ex-clients.
Friends.
Family.
Professional groups.
Community groups.
Referral chains.
Recruitment candidates.
Sales prospects.

### Relationship Activation is both

### Evidence
Contact attempts, completed calls, booked appointments, referral asks.

### Interpretation
Activation rate, activation quality, network expansion quality, relationship exhaustion risk.


## 3. Activation Events

3.1 Fact Events

### Contact_attempted
### Meaning
A person attempted to contact a relationship node.

### Contact_completed
### Meaning
Contact actually occurred.

### Appointment_requested
### Meaning
An appointment or interview was requested.

### Appointment_booked
### Meaning
An appointment or interview was scheduled.

### Referral_requested
### Meaning
A referral was requested from a relationship node.

### Referral_received
### Meaning
A referral/name/introduction was received.

### Magic_question_asked
### Meaning
Magic Question or equivalent referral-expansion question was asked.

### Ci_contacted
### Meaning
Center of Influence was contacted.

### Introduction_requested
### Meaning
An introduction to another person/group was requested.

### Introduction_received
### Meaning
The introduction happened or was provided.

### Followup_completed
### Meaning
Follow-up activity was completed.

### Reconnection_completed
### Meaning
A dormant/stale relationship was reconnected.

### Network_expansion_event
### Meaning
Relationship activation produced new names, introductions, referrals or groups.

### P200_contact_activated
### Meaning
A P200 relationship was acted on.

### Market_cluster_activated
### Meaning
A market cluster or community group was intentionally activated.


3.2 Interpretation Events

### Relationship_activation_rate_updated
### Meaning
Activation ratio was evaluated.

### Activation_quality_evaluated
### Meaning
Activation quality was interpreted from outcomes.

### Network_expansion_quality_evaluated
### Meaning
Expansion value was interpreted.

### Relationship_exhaustion_risk_detected
### Meaning
Forge detects possible overuse, decay or saturation.

### Warm_market_underactivated
### Meaning
Relationship Capital exists but is not being used.

### Trust_transfer_opportunity_detected
### Meaning
Forge identifies a trust path that could improve conversion.


3.3 Activity Events

Activity events are facts of execution, but their ownership may belong to Mick.

### Examples

### Call_planned.
### Call_completed.
### Message_sent.
### Followup_task_completed.
### Referral_ask_completed.
### Ci_touchpoint_completed.

Mick interprets discipline.
Relationship Activation interprets commercial use of relationship access.


3.4 Result Events

### Appointment_created.
### Interview_created.
### Referral_created.
### Introduction_created.
### Opportunity_created.
### Candidate_created.
### Client_opportunity_created.
### Network_node_created.

These are outcomes of activation.

They should not be confused with activation attempts.


## 4. Activation Vs Relationship Capital

### Why Relationship Capital is not enough

Relationship Capital is potential.

It can exist without action.
It can remain dormant.
It can decay.
It can be wasted.
It can be strong but unused.

### Relationship Capital tells Forge
There is access.

### It does not tell Forge
The access is being used.

### Why Market Natural is not enough

Market Natural reveals where natural access exists.

It does not guarantee contact, trust, appointment or referral.

A person may know many people and still not activate them.

### Why P200 is not enough

P200 externalizes declared Market Natural.

It is evidence of a relationship inventory.

### It does not prove

Contact.
Willingness.
Follow-up.
Conversion.
Appointment creation.
Referral creation.
Trust transfer.
Production.

### Clear difference

### Relationship Capital
Potential access.

### Market Natural
Reachable starting field.

### P200
Visible evidence of declared field.

### Activation
Observed use of the field.

### Result
Commercial movement produced by activation.


## 5. Activation Vs Mick

Mick measures behavior.

Relationship Activation measures the commercial use of relationship assets.

They overlap but are not the same.

Does Activation belong to Mick?

No, not exclusively.

### Mick can own behavior execution metrics

Calls completed.
Follow-ups completed.
Referral asks completed.
Consistency.
Cadence.
Discipline.
Avoidance.
Coachability.

### Relationship Activation owns or interprets

Which relationship asset was used.
Which relationship cluster was activated.
Which trust path was used.
Whether activation produced contact, appointment, referral, candidate or opportunity.
Whether Market Natural is dormant or active.
Whether activation is expanding or exhausting the network.

Is Activation consumed by Mick?

Yes.

Mick should consume activation facts to evaluate discipline and behavior quality.

Is Activation a domain independent?

Not yet.

It is too transversal and too dependent on Relationship Capital, Sales Prospecting, Recruitment and Mick.

Is Activation a subdomain?

Possibly later.

It could become a subdomain of Relationship Intelligence, Revenue Generation, or a transversal capability.

### Current decision
Relationship Activation is a transversal capability and interpretation layer.

Is Activation simply evidence?

No.

Activation includes evidence, but also interpretation.

### Evidence
Call happened.
Referral asked.
Introduction received.

### Interpretation
Relationship asset is underactivated.
CI activation is high quality.
Warm market is decaying.

### Ownership

### Execution behavior
Mick.

### Relationship asset context
Relationship Capital / Shared Commercial Model primitives.

### Recruitment use
Recruitment Intelligence.

### Sales use
Sales Prospecting / Revenue Generation.

### Cross-domain activation interpretation
Relationship Activation capability.


## 6. Activation Patterns

6.1 P200 to Call

### Pattern
P200 Evidence
Relationship selected
Contact attempted
Contact completed
Next action created

### Universal
Yes.

### Appears in
Sales prospecting.
Recruitment.
Relationship reactivation.


6.2 P200 to Appointment

### Pattern
P200 Evidence
Contact completed
Appointment requested
Appointment booked

### Universal
Yes.

### Appears in
Sales.
Recruitment.


6.3 PM to New Name

### Pattern
Relationship interaction
Magic Question asked
Referral received
New relationship node created

### Universal
Yes, with domain-specific wording.

### Appears in
Recruitment.
Sales referrals.
Client referrals.


6.4 CI to Introduction

### Pattern
CI identified
CI contacted
Introduction requested
Introduction received
New group/person accessed

### Universal
Yes.

### Appears in
Recruitment.
Sales prospecting.
Partner development.


6.5 Client to Referral

### Pattern
Client relationship
Trust established
Referral requested
Referral received
New opportunity created

### Universal
Yes.

### Appears in
Sales.
Recruitment if client refers candidate.


6.6 Ex-client to Reactivation

### Pattern
Dormant relationship
Reconnection attempted
Reconnection completed
Opportunity or referral identified

### Universal
Yes.

### Appears in
Sales.
Relationship Intelligence.
Revenue Intelligence.


6.7 Market Cluster Activation

### Pattern
Cluster identified
Influence node selected
Touchpoint completed
Group access created
Multiple opportunities generated

### Universal
Yes.

### Appears in
Sales.

Partner growth.


6.8 Common layer across sales and recruitment

### Universal activation layer

Relationship selected.
Trust path identified.
Contact attempted.
Contact completed.
Ask made.
Introduction/referral/appointment created.
Follow-up completed.
Network expanded.

### What changes

The desired outcome changes by domain.

### Sales outcome
Prospect, appointment, client, policy, referral.

### Recruitment outcome
Candidate, interview, connected advisor, signed advisor, referral.


## 7. Trust Transfer Connection

### Proposed chain

Relationship Capital
Activation
Trust Transfer
Opportunity

### Assessment
Mostly correct, but incomplete.

### Better chain

Relationship Capital
Trust Path
Activation
Trust Transfer
Attention / Access
Opportunity
Conversion

### Role of Activation

Activation turns a passive trust path into an active commercial interaction.

Without activation, trust remains latent.

### Role of PM

PM activates a current relationship to generate new relationship nodes.

It converts trust into network expansion.

### Role of CI

CI activates influence.

CI can transfer trust from a respected node to a group or individual.

### Role of referrals

Referrals move trust from one relationship to a new relationship.

Trust transfer does not guarantee conversion.

### It improves

Attention.
Willingness to listen.
Initial credibility.
Lower friction.
Higher probability of appointment.

### It does not guarantee

Need.
Fit.
Budget.
Eligibility.
Commitment.
Production.


## 8. Sales Vs Recruitment

### Sales flow

Market Natural
Relationship selected
Contact
Appointment
Needs discovery
Solution
Client
Referral

### Recruitment flow

Market Natural
Relationship selected
Contact
Interview
Evaluation
Connected
Signed
Development
Referral

### Common layer

Relationship Activation.

### Shared primitives

CommercialPerson.
CommercialRelationship.
CommercialAccount.
CommercialAttribution.
EvidenceRecord.
ProvenanceRecord.
PeriodSnapshot.

### Shared activation steps

Identify relationship.
Choose trust path.
Attempt contact.
Complete contact.
Ask for meeting/interview/referral.
Book meeting/interview.
Follow up.
Expand network.

### What changes

Sales uses activation to create client and revenue opportunities.

Recruitment uses activation to create candidates and future advisor capacity.

### Boundary decision

Relationship Activation is a shared capability used by both Sales Prospecting and Recruitment Intelligence.

It should not be owned by either one exclusively.


## 9. Activation Metrics

9.1 Valid metrics

### Relationship Activation Rate
Activated relationships / available relationship inventory.

### P200 Activation Rate
P200 names contacted or acted on / P200 names available.

### Warm Contact Rate
Warm relationships contacted / warm relationships available.

### Contact Completion Rate
Completed contacts / attempted contacts.

### Appointment Request Rate
Appointment requests / completed contacts.

### Appointment Creation Rate
Appointments booked / completed contacts.

### Referral Ask Rate
Referral asks / eligible relationship interactions.

### Referral Received Rate
Referrals received / referral asks.

### Magic Question Ask Rate
Magic Question asked / eligible recruitment interviews.

### Magic Question Yield
New names from Magic Question / Magic Questions asked.

### CI Activation Rate
CI touchpoints completed / active CI relationships.

### Introduction Request Rate
Introductions requested / CI or referral opportunities.

### Introduction Received Rate
Introductions received / introductions requested.

### Network Expansion Rate
New relationship nodes created / activation interactions.

### Reconnection Rate
Dormant relationships reconnected / dormant relationships targeted.

### Activation to Opportunity Rate
Opportunities created / activated relationships.

### Activation to Candidate Rate
Candidates created / activated relationships.

### Activation to Client Prospect Rate
Sales prospects created / activated relationships.

### Cluster Activation Rate
Activated clusters / identified Market Natural clusters.

### Activation Freshness
Time since last meaningful activation.


9.2 Vanity metrics

Raw calls without completed contact.
Messages sent without response.
P200 count without activation.
Referral asks without received referrals.
PM asked without quality or conversion.
CI contacts without introductions.
Network expansion count without downstream movement.
Appointments requested but not booked.
Follow-up tasks created but not completed.
Activation volume without trust path.
Activation volume without outcomes.


9.3 Metric ownership

### Mick owns
Execution behavior and consistency.

### Relationship Activation owns
Activation interpretation and relationship-use metrics.

### Recruitment owns
Recruitment activation outcomes such as candidate/interview creation.

### Sales Prospecting owns
Sales activation outcomes such as appointments/prospects.

### Business Planning consumes
Activation metrics for feasibility and action planning.

### Partner Intelligence consumes
Activation metrics for advisor unit viability and coaching.


## 10. Red Team Review

### Scenario 1
High activation and zero results.

### Explanation
Activation alone is not enough.
Relationships may be weak, message may be poor, timing may be wrong, offer may be unclear, or market fit may be low.

### Limit
Activation is necessary but not sufficient.

### Guardrail
Measure activation quality and downstream conversion.


### Scenario 2
Low activation and many results.

### Explanation
Few high-quality relationships, strong CI, strong referrals or high trust may produce results with low volume.

### Limit
Volume is not the same as effectiveness.

### Guardrail
Measure quality, trust transfer and conversion.


### Scenario 3
Activation over weak relationships.

### Explanation
Many attempts can generate low response and possible fatigue.

### Limit
Activation quality depends on relationship strength.

### Guardrail
Use relationship quality and trust path context.


### Scenario 4
Activation over strong CI.

### Explanation
Can create high leverage and multiple opportunities.

### Limit
CI can become exhausted or damaged if overused.

### Guardrail
Track CI freshness, reciprocity, quality and relationship health.


### Scenario 5
Excessive activation damages relationships.

### Explanation
Too many asks, weak timing or transactional behavior can reduce trust.

### Limit
Activation can destroy Relationship Capital.

### Guardrail
Relationship Health and trust preservation must constrain activation recommendations.


### Scenario 6
Frequent PM with low quality.

### Explanation
The ask happens but generated names are weak.

### Limit
PM count is not PM value.

### Guardrail
Measure PM yield and conversion.


### Scenario 7
High contact with no trust.

### Explanation
Cold or weak-trust contact may produce low conversion.

### Limit
Activation without trust transfer has lower quality.

### Guardrail
Separate warm activation from cold activation.


### Scenario 8
High trust with no action.

### Explanation
Relationship Capital exists but remains latent.

### Limit
Trust is not outcome.

### Guardrail
Detect underactivation.


### Red Team conclusion

Relationship Activation is real but cannot be treated as guaranteed productivity.

### It must be connected to

Relationship quality.
Trust transfer.
Message quality.
Follow-up.
Domain outcome.
Conversion.
Relationship health.


## 11. Foundation Impact

11.1 CommercialPerson

### Impact
Activation events happen between or through CommercialPerson nodes.

Do not embed activation as a permanent person attribute.


11.2 CommercialRelationship

### Impact
CommercialRelationship must support activation history, relationship freshness and trust path context.

Do not confuse relationship existence with relationship activation.


11.3 CommercialAttribution

### Impact
### Activation may create attribution

Who introduced.
Who referred.
Who activated.
Who created the opportunity.

### Guardrail
Attribution does not imply compensation without Rule Pack.


11.4 Relationship Capital

### Impact
Relationship Capital becomes measurable through activation and outcomes.

### Guardrail
Relationship Capital is still the asset; activation is use of the asset.


11.5 Market Natural

### Impact
Market Natural quality must be evaluated through activation potential and activation outcomes, not only P200 size.


11.6 P200

### Impact
P200 becomes useful only when activated.

### Valid derivative
P200 Activation Snapshot.

### Invalid derivative
P200 Completion = productivity.


11.7 Recruitment Intelligence

### Impact
Recruitment should consume activation events to identify candidates, interviews, PM yield and recruiting risk.

Recruitment does not own activation globally.


11.8 Sales Prospecting

### Impact
Sales Prospecting should consume activation events to identify appointments, prospects, referrals and client opportunities.

Sales does not own activation globally.


11.9 Partner Intelligence

### Impact
Partner Intelligence should use activation to evaluate whether advisors are becoming viable economic units.

### It should ask

Is the advisor activating Market Natural?
Is the advisor expanding the network?
Is the advisor converting relationship access into appointments/interviews/opportunities?


11.10 Business Planning

### Impact
Business Planning should use activation metrics to test plan feasibility.

A plan requiring 20 appointments is unrealistic if activation rate and relationship inventory cannot support it.


11.11 Mick

### Impact
Mick consumes activation behavior to evaluate discipline, consistency and avoidance.

Mick should not own all activation meaning.


## 12. Architecture Decision

### Relationship Activation is

### Concept
Yes.

### Capability
Yes.

### Domain
No, not now.

### Subdomain
Possible later, but not approved now.

### Asset
No.

Activation uses an asset.
It is not the asset.

### Interpretation
Yes.

### Evidence
Partly.

Raw activation events are evidence.
Activation quality and activation health are interpretations.

### Decision
APPROVED

### Approved as

Transversal capability.
Interpretation layer.
Shared activation concept between Sales Prospecting, Recruitment, Relationship Intelligence, Partner Intelligence, Business Planning and Mick.

### Not approved as

Standalone domain.
Forge Core primitive.
Implementation.
Schema.
Engine.

### Why

The concept is necessary to explain why identical Relationship Capital can produce different outcomes.

It prevents Forge from confusing potential with action.

It connects relationship assets to real commercial movement.


## 13. Recommended Next Step

## Recommended Next Step
Recruitment Hardening.

### Why

Recruitment is already ARCHITECTURE CANDIDATE.
PAQ-03 and PAQ-04 are locked.
This PAQ clarifies the missing activation layer.

### Recruitment Hardening can now safely use

Relationship Capital.
Market Natural.
P200 Evidence.
Relationship Activation.
Trust Transfer.
Recruitment Funnel.

### Why not Partner Intelligence next

Partner Intelligence depends on hardened recruitment and activation semantics.

### Why not Productivity Intelligence next

Productivity depends on understanding whether relationship assets are activated before interpreting output.

### Why not Forecast Intelligence next

Forecast needs activation metrics and recruitment metrics stabilized first.

### Why not Business Planning next

Business Planning needs validated activation metrics to avoid unrealistic plans.


## 14. Final Verdict

Relationship Activation is the missing bridge between potential relationships and actual results.

### Final architecture chain

Relationship Capital
Market Natural
P200 Evidence
Relationship Activation
Trust Transfer
Opportunity
Outcome

Relationship Capital does not produce results by itself.

Market Natural does not produce results by itself.

P200 does not produce results by itself.

Activation converts relationship potential into commercial motion.

### Activation can create

Contact.
Appointment.
Interview.
Referral.
Introduction.
Opportunity.
Candidate.
Client prospect.
Network expansion.

Relationship Activation should be APPROVED as a transversal capability and interpretation layer.

It should not become a standalone domain yet.

It should be consumed by Recruitment Intelligence, Sales Prospecting, Partner Intelligence, Business Planning, Relationship Intelligence, Forecast Intelligence and Mick.

### The next architecture move remains

Recruitment Hardening.

### Recruitment Hardening must incorporate this rule

Recruitment does not begin with P200.
Recruitment begins when Market Natural or Relationship Capital is activated for the purpose of creating candidate flow.



===== PAQ-06-RECRUITMENT-HARDENING-REVIEW.md =====

# PAQ-06 Recruitment Hardening Review

## Repository References

- [FORGE_MASTER_BUILD_TREE.md](FORGE_MASTER_BUILD_TREE.md)
- [AGENTS.md](AGENTS.md)
- [FORGE_CONSTITUTION_V3.md](FORGE_CONSTITUTION_V3.md)
- [FORGE_FOUNDATION_LOCK.md](FORGE_FOUNDATION_LOCK.md)

---


Forge OS
Principal Domain Architect Review
Recruitment Intelligence Hardening
Codename: Andrey Garcia

### Status
ARCHITECTURE LOCK RECOMMENDED

### Scope
Architecture only.
No code.
No engines.
No schemas.
No UI.
No commits.


## 1. Executive Summary

Recruitment Intelligence is the Forge domain responsible for explaining whether a Partner, manager or commercial organization is creating enough future advisor capacity through candidate flow.

It does not begin with Relationship Capital.
It does not begin with Market Natural.
It does not begin with P200.

Recruitment Intelligence consumes those layers.

Recruitment begins when an existing or discovered relationship is activated with explicit candidate-generation intent.

### The hardened causal boundary is

Relationship Capital
Market Natural
P200 Evidence
Relationship Activation
Candidate Flow
Recruitment Funnel
Precontract Handoff

Recruitment Intelligence exists because future commercial growth does not start with compensation, productivity or production. It starts earlier, when the organization generates enough viable candidates who can become advisors.

### The operating phrase

"Si reclutas, nada mas importa.
Si no reclutas, nada mas importa."

is not a slogan inside Forge.

Architecturally, it means:

If candidate flow is insufficient, later domains will starve.
If candidate quality is poor, development will absorb the failure.
If source quality is weak, forecast confidence declines.
If recruitment stops, future productivity risk increases.

### Recruitment Intelligence answers

Do I have enough candidate flow?
Where is candidate flow coming from?
Which sources are producing viable candidates?
Where does the funnel break?
Which candidates are stuck?
Which conversion is deteriorating?
Which Partner is creating future advisor capacity?
Which recruitment behavior predicts future shortage?
What recruitment gap threatens future productivity?

### Recruitment Intelligence enables decisions such as

Activate more warm sources.
Re-engage Centers of Influence.
Ask more Magic Questions.
Reduce dependence on cold sources.
Coach a Partner on interview conversion.
Prioritize stuck candidates.
Protect future productivity by restoring candidate flow.

### Final hardening conclusion

Recruitment Intelligence is ready for ARCHITECTURE LOCK at the domain-boundary level.

SMNYL Agency 2026 recruitment vocabulary, stages and thresholds belong to the Rule Pack.
Forge Core must only preserve the universal primitives, events, ownership and interpretation boundaries.


## 2. Recruitment Definition

### Recruitment Intelligence is

The domain that transforms activated relationship access into measured candidate flow, funnel conversion, recruitment risk and future advisor capacity.

It explains whether the organization is consistently creating enough potential advisors, from the right sources, with enough quality, at the right pace, to sustain future growth.

### Recruitment Intelligence starts when

A relationship, market contact, referred person, Center of Influence, Magic Question result, nominated person, observed person or cold contact is activated with the specific intent of generating a candidate for the advisor career.

### Recruitment Intelligence ends when

The candidate reaches the formal handoff into Precontract, or the candidate exits, stalls, is disqualified or is abandoned.

Recruitment Intelligence may consume downstream signed outcomes because signed outcomes validate upstream recruitment quality.

However, Recruitment Intelligence does not own the full Precontract lifecycle, advisor contract state, development process, productivity, compensation or career progression.

### Recruitment Intelligence is not

Relationship Capital.
Market Natural.
P200.
Generic Sales Prospecting.
Relationship Activation as a whole.
Precontract Intelligence.
Development Intelligence.
Productivity Intelligence.
Compensation Intelligence.
Forecast Intelligence as a whole.
Business Planning Intelligence.
Partner Intelligence as a whole.

Recruitment Intelligence is not merely "reclutamiento" as an administrative activity.

### It is a decision intelligence domain that explains

Candidate flow.
Candidate source quality.
Interview conversion.
Pipeline health.
Recruitment risk.
Future advisor capacity.
Recruitment contribution to Partner growth.

### Universal definition

Recruitment Intelligence owns the interpretation of candidate-generation activity after relationship activation and before formal precontract ownership.

### Rule Pack definition

Specific labels such as EI, ES, EC, EA, Conectado, Firmado, NOM, CI, RDA, OP, PM, FF and any qualifying thresholds belong to the active Rule Pack.

Forge Core must not hardcode those meanings as universal business law.


## 3. Recruitment Inputs

Recruitment Intelligence consumes the following inputs.

It does not own all of them.


Relationship Capital

### Consume
Yes.

### Ownership
Not Recruitment.
Relationship Capital is an approved transversal concept and shared asset model.

### Dependency
Recruitment uses Relationship Capital to understand available social, professional, client, referral and community access that can be activated for candidate generation.

### Recruitment interpretation
Which relationship assets are being converted into candidate flow?

### Recruitment must not
Treat Relationship Capital as a recruitment list.
Reduce Relationship Capital to names.
Assume a large relationship network implies strong recruitment capacity.


Market Natural

### Consume
Yes.

### Ownership
Not Recruitment.
Market Natural is an approved conceptual layer inside Relationship Capital.

### Dependency
Recruitment uses Market Natural to understand the reachable starting field from which candidates may emerge.

### Recruitment interpretation
Is the Partner using the natural market to generate candidates?
Which market clusters are producing candidate opportunities?

### Recruitment must not
Own Market Natural.
Treat Market Natural as a recruitment-only concept.
Treat Market Natural as proof of candidate quality.


P200 Evidence

### Consume
Yes.

### Ownership
Not Recruitment.
P200 is a Market Natural Discovery Artifact.

### Dependency
Recruitment consumes P200 as evidence of declared relationship inventory, market clusters and potential activation surface.

### Recruitment interpretation
Which P200 relationships have been activated for recruitment?
Which P200 clusters produce candidates?
Which P200 areas remain unused?

### Recruitment must not
Own P200.
Treat P200 as a candidate list.
Treat P200 completion as recruitment success.
Treat 200 names as proof of strong Market Natural.


Relationship Activation

### Consume
Yes.

### Ownership
Not exclusively Recruitment.
Relationship Activation is an approved transversal capability.

### Dependency
Recruitment uses activation events when the activation intent is candidate generation.

### Recruitment interpretation
Which activated relationships became candidate opportunities?
Which activation patterns produce interviews, connected candidates or signed advisors?

### Recruitment must not
Own all activation behavior.
Confuse activation volume with recruitment quality.


Trust Transfer

### Consume
Yes.

### Ownership
Principle candidate, not exclusive domain ownership.

### Dependency
Recruitment uses Trust Transfer to explain why some sources produce higher quality candidate movement.

### Recruitment interpretation
Which candidate sources carry transferred trust?
Which sources require cold conversion effort?

### Recruitment must not
Assume trust transfer guarantees quality.
Treat warm sources as automatically superior without conversion evidence.


Referral Events

### Consume
Yes.

### Ownership
Shared event taxonomy and Relationship Intelligence may own broader relationship referral semantics.
Recruitment owns recruitment-specific candidate interpretation.

### Dependency
Recruitment consumes referral events when the referred person enters candidate flow.

### Recruitment interpretation
Which referrals became candidates?
Which referrers generate viable candidate flow?


CI Events

### Consume
Yes.

### Ownership
Relationship Capital / Relationship Intelligence own the broader CI relationship.
Recruitment owns recruitment interpretation when CI generates candidate flow.

### Dependency
Recruitment consumes CI contact, introduction and referral events when used for candidate generation.

### Recruitment interpretation
Which Centers of Influence create candidate access?
Which CI relationships are underused?


Magic Question Events

### Consume
Yes.

### Ownership
The Magic Question pattern is not exclusively Recruitment.
It appears in recruitment and sales prospecting.

### Dependency
Recruitment consumes Magic Question events when the question creates or attempts to create candidate referrals.

### Recruitment interpretation
Which candidates or interviewees generate new candidate names?
What is the yield and quality of PM-sourced candidates?

### Recruitment must not
Treat PM as only a source code.
Ignore the network expansion pattern behind PM.


Partner Context

### Consume
Yes.

### Ownership
Partner Intelligence owns partner-level interpretation.
CommercialAssignment owns historical assignment context.

### Dependency
Recruitment needs Partner context to attribute candidate flow, pipeline health and recruitment risk.

### Recruitment interpretation
Which Partner is generating candidate flow?
Which Partner has future advisor capacity risk?


Candidate Context

Consume and own partially.

### Ownership
CommercialPerson owns durable person identity.
Recruitment Intelligence owns recruitment candidate context, stage history, source attribution and funnel interpretation.

### Dependency
Recruitment needs person identity, relationship origin, source evidence, activity history and stage movement.

### Recruitment must not
Create duplicate person identity.
Overwrite historical candidate attempts.
Treat candidateId as durable human identity.


## 4. Recruitment Outputs

Recruitment Intelligence produces the following outputs.


Candidate

Recruitment produces a candidate context.

### This means

A CommercialPerson or potential CommercialPerson has entered candidate-generation flow.

### Recruitment owns
RecruitmentCandidate context.
Candidate source.
Candidate stage.
Candidate funnel history.
Recruitment-specific risk.

### Recruitment does not own
Permanent person identity.

Contract state.

Stage-specific criteria.


Connected

### Precontract owns
The lifecycle after connection.
Precontract cycle.
Precontract rules.
Precontract readiness.
Precontract failure/success mechanics.


Signed

Recruitment does not own the official contract event.

### Recruitment uses signed outcomes to evaluate

Future advisor capacity.
Recruitment effectiveness.

### Career or Precontract owns
Official contract state.
Career Month start.
Advisor conversion.


Future Advisor Capacity

Recruitment produces an interpretation of potential future advisor supply.

It is not a guaranteed forecast.

### It is based on

Active candidates.
Source quality.
Stage distribution.
Conversion history.
Pipeline aging.
Connected count.
Signed outcomes.
Rule Pack context.

### Consumers
Partner Intelligence.

Advisor Development.


Recruitment Risk

Inactive Centers of Influence.
Stage conversion collapse.

Recruitment inactivity.


Recruitment Forecast

Recruitment owns recruitment-domain forecasts.

### Examples

Probable EI count.
Probable ES count.
Probable EC count.
Probable EA count.
Probable connected candidates.
Probable signed candidates.
Candidate flow shortage.
Source yield trend.

Forecast Intelligence owns cross-domain forecast orchestration.

Recruitment forecasts must always remain suggestions.
They are not facts.


Candidate Pipeline

Recruitment owns Candidate Pipeline.

### Candidate Pipeline includes

Candidates by stage.
Candidates by source.
Candidates by Partner.
Candidates by age in stage.
Candidates by activation path.
Candidates by risk.
Candidates by next required action.

### Candidate Pipeline does not include

General Relationship Capital.
General P200 inventory.
Sales opportunities.
Production pipeline.
Compensation pipeline.

### Important downstream boundary

### What does not belong inside the recruitment funnel

P200 completion.

Advisor productivity.
Compensation.
Alta Partner.

### Recruitment funnel principle

Recruitment is not the existence of names.
Recruitment is the conversion of activated relationships into candidate movement.

## 7. Event Model Hardening

Recruitment events must obey the Commercial Events Taxonomy.

Facts are not interpretations.
Forecasts are not facts.
Decisions are not facts.
Snapshots are not events unless they record a specific state capture.


Fact Events

### Candidate_identified

### Represents
A person has been identified as a possible candidate.

### Does not represent
Quality.
Probability.
Eligibility.


### Candidate_created

### Represents
A recruitment candidate context was opened.

### Does not represent
Advisor identity.
Contract state.


### Candidate_source_assigned

### Represents
A source was assigned to the candidate.

### Does not represent
Source quality.


### Candidate_referred

### Represents
Candidate came through a referral path.

### Does not represent
Guaranteed trust or quality.


### Ci_introduction_received

### Represents
A Center of Influence provided an introduction or access.

### Does not represent
Candidate acceptance.


### Magic_question_referral_created

### Represents
A Magic Question produced a referred name.

### Does not represent
Candidate quality.


### Contact_attempted

### Represents
Contact was attempted.

### Does not represent
Connection, interest or quality.


### Contact_completed

### Represents
Contact was completed.

### Does not represent
Interview qualification.


### Ei_scheduled
### Ei_completed
### Es_scheduled
### Es_completed
### Ec_scheduled
### Ec_completed
### Ea_scheduled
### Ea_completed

### Represent
Recruitment stage scheduling and completion facts.

### Do not represent
Automatic advancement unless the Rule Pack says so.


### Candidate_advanced

### Represents
Candidate moved to a next recruitment stage.

### Does not represent
Final success.


### Candidate_stalled

### Represents
Candidate has not moved within expected operational timing.

This may be fact or interpretation depending on whether the stall threshold comes from Rule Pack or operational policy.


### Candidate_disqualified

### Represents
Candidate was removed from active recruitment for a stated reason.

### Does not represent
Permanent impossibility.


### Candidate_abandoned

### Represents
Candidate exited or stopped responding.

### Does not represent
Cause unless cause evidence exists.


### Candidate_reactivated

### Represents
Candidate re-entered active recruitment flow.

### Does not erase
Prior history.


### Precontract_started

### Represents
Recruitment reached precontract handoff.

### Ownership
Boundary event.


### Contract_signed

### Represents
Official signing occurred.

### Ownership
Downstream lifecycle.

Recruitment consumes it.


Interpretation Events

### Source_quality_evaluated

### Represents
Recruitment interpreted source quality from evidence and conversion.


### Funnel_gap_detected

### Represents
Recruitment identified a conversion break.


### Warm_source_shortage_detected

### Represents
Recruitment identified insufficient warm source generation.


### Cold_source_overreliance_detected

### Represents
Recruitment identified dependency on cold sources.


### Pm_quality_evaluated

### Represents
Magic Question output was evaluated by quality, not only volume.


### Future_advisor_capacity_evaluated

### Represents
Recruitment interpreted whether current candidate flow can support future advisor capacity.


### Recruitment_risk_detected

### Represents
Recruitment risk was identified.


Decision Events

### Candidate_advance_decided
### Candidate_hold_decided
### Candidate_stop_decided
### Followup_required
### Source_activation_required
### Magic_question_required
### Ci_reactivation_required
### Manager_coaching_required
### Precontract_handoff_ready

These are decisions or recommended decisions.
They are not facts unless executed.


Experience Events

### Recruitment_help_shown
### Source_quality_explained
### Funnel_causal_chain_explained
### Recruitment_risk_explained
### Next_action_explained

These support Advisor Experience, Clippy, Learning Through Reasoning and Causal Clarity.


System Events

### Duplicate_candidate_detected
### Candidate_record_merged
### Source_evidence_attached
### Excel_import_reviewed
### Recruitment_snapshot_created
### Rule_pack_applied
### Rule_pack_version_changed

These support integrity, provenance and auditability.


Events that do not belong to Recruitment

P200_COMPLETED as recruitment success.
### Policy_paid.
### Commission_paid.
### Ta_qualified.
### Advisor_productivity_updated.
### Bonus_calculated.
### Limra_updated.
### Igc_updated.

Recruitment may consume downstream outcomes for validation.
It does not own them.


## 8. Source Intelligence Hardening

Source Intelligence inside Recruitment must evaluate both volume and quality.

Source count alone is not sufficient.


NOM

### Meaning
Nominados.

### Semantics
Named people nominated or identified through known context.

### Typical warmth
Medium to warm, depending on who nominated and why.

### Trust transfer
Possible, but not automatic.

### Strength
Can produce candidate flow when nomination carries context and credibility.

### Weakness
May become a raw-name bucket without activation or quality.

### Expected conversion
Should outperform pure cold source when nomination contains real relational context.

### Risk
Inflated nomination volume without candidate movement.

### Leading indicators
NOM-to-EI conversion.
NOM source freshness.
NOM trust path clarity.


CI

### Meaning
Centro de Influencia.

### Semantics
A person or node with influence, credibility and access to a community or group.

### Typical warmth
High potential warmth.

### Trust transfer
High when CI credibility is real and introduction is direct.

### Strength
Can open access to multiple candidates or communities.

### Weakness
CI can stop referring, provide low-fit names or become inactive.

### Expected conversion
Should be measured by introduced candidates, EI conversion, connected conversion and signed quality.

### Risk
Treating CI count as value without introductions or outcomes.

### Leading indicators
Active CI count.
CI contact recency.
CI introduction rate.
CI-to-EI conversion.
CI-to-connected conversion.


RDA

### Meaning
Referido de Asesor.

### Semantics
Candidate referred by an advisor.

### Typical warmth
Warm when advisor credibility transfers.

### Trust transfer
Medium to high depending on advisor relationship and credibility.

### Strength
Can produce candidates with clearer career context.

### Weakness
Advisor may refer for obligation, not quality.

### Expected conversion
Should be measured by referred-to-interview and referred-to-connected conversion.

### Risk
Advisor referral volume without quality.

### Leading indicators
RDA-to-EI conversion.
RDA-to-connected conversion.
RDA source advisor quality.


OP

### Meaning
Observacion Personal.

### Semantics
Person identified by direct observation.

### Typical warmth
Variable.

### Trust transfer
Low to medium unless relationship exists.

### Strength
Can identify talent outside existing circles.

### Weakness
May rely on subjective impression without evidence.

### Expected conversion
Variable, should be validated by stage movement.

### Risk
False positives based on appearance, confidence or superficial traits.

### Leading indicators
OP-to-contact completion.
OP-to-EI conversion.
OP drop reason pattern.


PM

### Meaning
Pregunta Magica.

### Semantics
Network expansion pattern that asks an interviewee or contact who they would invite to a similar opportunity.

### Typical warmth
Variable.

### Trust transfer
Depends on the relationship between referrer and referred person.

### Strength
Creates candidate network loops.

### Weakness
Can generate many names with low quality if asked mechanically.

### Expected conversion
Must be evaluated by yield and candidate quality, not PM count.

### Risk
Treating PM as only a source code.

### Leading indicators
PM ask rate.
PM names per ask.
PM-to-EI conversion.
PM-to-connected conversion.
PM referral depth.


FF

### Meaning
Fuente Fria.

### Semantics
Cold source with little or no prior trust path.

### Typical warmth
Low.

### Trust transfer
Low or absent.

### Strength
Can supplement pipeline when warm sources are insufficient.

### Weakness
Usually higher friction and lower trust.

### Expected conversion
Must be measured separately from warm sources.

### Risk
High FF dependency can hide weak Relationship Capital activation.

### Leading indicators
FF ratio.
FF-to-EI conversion.
FF-to-connected conversion.
Cost or effort per viable candidate.


Source Intelligence rules

Warm source ratio is more important than raw source count.
Trust path clarity is more important than source label.
Source-to-stage conversion is more important than source volume.
Source quality must be learned from outcomes.
Forge must not assume a source is good without evidence.


## 9. Conversion Intelligence

Recruitment conversion must explain movement between stages, not merely count completed activities.


EI to ES

### Meaning
Initial interview produced enough fit, interest or qualification to continue.

### Decision enabled
Improve initial filtering.
Improve invitation quality.
Coach first interview execution.
Review source quality.

### Risk revealed
Many EI with few ES suggests poor initial qualification, weak positioning, wrong audience or interview quality issue.

### Valid metrics
EI count.
EI-to-ES conversion.
EI no-show rate.
EI source distribution.
EI age from candidate creation.

### Vanity metrics
EI count without ES conversion.


ES to EC

### Meaning
Selection interview produced enough seriousness or career fit to proceed to career conversation.

### Decision enabled
Review candidate motivation.
Improve selection criteria.
Coach selection conversation.

### Risk revealed
Many ES with few EC suggests weak career fit, unclear expectations or poor candidate readiness.

### Valid metrics
ES-to-EC conversion.
ES drop reasons.
Time from ES to EC.
Source-specific ES-to-EC conversion.

### Vanity metrics
ES volume without EC outcomes.


EC to EA

### Meaning
Career interview produced enough conviction or interest to justify additional interview.

### Decision enabled
Improve career explanation.
Clarify economic opportunity.
Coach career storytelling.

### Risk revealed
Many EC with few EA suggests weak career case, poor economic clarity or candidate mismatch.

### Valid metrics
EC-to-EA conversion.
EC objection patterns.
EC stage aging.
EC source-specific conversion.

### Vanity metrics
EC count without EA movement.


EA to Connected

### Meaning
Additional interview produced enough commitment to begin Precontract.

### Decision enabled
Prioritize close follow-up.
Identify readiness barriers.
Coach final commitment conversation.

### Risk revealed
Many EA with few connected suggests late-stage friction, weak commitment, unclear requirements or operational delay.

### Valid metrics
EA-to-connected conversion.
Time from EA to connected.
Late-stage drop reason.
Connected readiness quality.

### Vanity metrics
EA count without connected movement.


Connected to Signed

### Meaning
Candidate who began Precontract signed contract.

### Ownership
Recruitment consumes this outcome.
Precontract and Career own official process and state.

### Decision enabled
Validate recruitment quality.
Identify precontract bottleneck.
Separate recruitment failure from development or precontract failure.

### Risk revealed
Many connected with few signed suggests precontract execution issue, expectation mismatch or weak candidate commitment.

### Valid metrics
