Forge Core never hardcodes carrier, channel, contest, compensation, career, promotion, KPI, activity or recognition logic.

### The hierarchy is now explicit

Carrier
Distribution Channel
Rule Pack
Rules

This hierarchy absorbs the operational specificity found in agency documents without contaminating Forge Core.


### Riesgos Importantes

1. Rule Pack boundary discipline.

### Risk
Future builders may accidentally place SMNYL-specific terms into Core.

### Examples
Prima Meta.
Bono Inicial.
Bono Renovación.
Bono GMM.
Training Allowance.
Productividad.
Apoyos.
Alta Partner.
MP1B.
MP1C.
MP2.
P200.
One Thing.

### Assessment
Important but not foundation-blocking. The foundation already states that these belong to Rule Packs or operational interpretation layers, not Core.


2. Language contamination risk.

### Risk
Because SMNYL Agency 2026 is the first validated Rule Pack, its language may become the default vocabulary.

### Assessment
Important. The foundation must preserve universal names in Core and allow Rule Pack-specific aliases.

### Core should speak in universal primitives

ProductionEvent.
RuleSnapshot.
MetricSnapshot.
PeriodSnapshot.
CommercialPerson.
CommercialAccount.
CommercialAttribution.
CommercialAssignment.
CommercialServicing.

### Rule Packs may speak in carrier/channel language

MP1B.
MP1C.
MP2.
P200.
TA.
Productividad.
Conexión.
Desarrollo.


3. Operational documents may mix rule, metric, process and coaching.

### Risk
Agency files such as Planeación Trimestral Partners, One Thing, P200 and Precont can contain rules, activities, goals, process guidance, coaching language and recognition criteria in the same artifact.

### Assessment
Important. Evidence & Provenance Foundation and Rule Snapshot Hardening are sufficient to handle this, but Rule Pack construction must classify each extracted item correctly.


4. Recruitment and productivity language may be carrier/channel-specific.

### Risk
Recruitment, P200, RTW, PM, Precont and planning materials may define activity expectations or productivity KPIs that should not become universal Core rules.

### Assessment
Important. The foundation handles this through Rule Packs, Metrics Ownership and Commercial Events. No foundation change required.


5. Multi-period interpretation risk.

### Risk
Quarterly planning, monthly productivity, campaign activity, recruitment cycles, precontract windows, contest periods and compensation payment periods can overlap.

### Assessment
Important. Periods & Operational Clocks Hardening is sufficient. No foundation change required.


6. Historical explanation depends on Rule Pack preservation.

### Risk
In 2032, Forge must explain why an advisor received or did not receive a 2026 SMNYL Agency bonus.

### Assessment
Important. RuleSnapshot Hardening and Evidence & Provenance Foundation are sufficient if Rule Pack snapshots preserve source documents and interpreted rule content.


7. Advisor Experience may surface Rule Pack-specific metrics.

### Risk
Benvenù, Clippy or Command OS could show carrier-specific metrics as if they are universal.

### Assessment
Important but controlled. Advisor Experience constraints already state that it consumes official owner snapshots and must not own business metrics.


8. Economic Motivation risk.

### Risk
Economic Motivation can overstate money if it consumes forecasts or unofficial Rule Pack interpretations.

### Assessment
Important. Metrics Ownership and Economic Motivation Guardrails are sufficient if enforced.


9. Event naming risk.

### Risk
Rule Pack-specific events may be confused with Core universal events.

### Assessment
Important. Commercial Events Taxonomy resolves the conceptual issue. Core events remain universal. Rule Pack outputs must be interpreted events or decision events scoped to the active Rule Pack.


10. Manager and Partner ambiguity.

### Risk
Partner Intelligence and Manager Intelligence may need different meanings across carriers and channels.

### Assessment
Important. Identity & Attribution Hardening is sufficient because it separates role, assignment, attribution and servicing.


### Riesgos Menores

1. Document naming inconsistency.

Some earlier documents use SMNYL terms directly.

### Assessment
Minor. This is a documentation hygiene issue, not a foundation defect, now that the Rule Pack boundary is explicit.


2. Mixed Spanish and English vocabulary.

### Assessment
Minor. Forge can support universal Core terms and Rule Pack-specific display labels.


3. Abbreviations in operational documents.

### Examples
MP2.
MP1B.
MP1C.
RTW.
PM.
P200.

### Assessment
Minor. These are Rule Pack or source-document terms. Evidence & Provenance can preserve their original language.


4. Future carrier variation.

AXA, GNP, MetLife and others may define different career, activity, contest and compensation structures.

### Assessment
Minor for foundation. This is exactly why Rule Packs exist.


5. User-facing simplicity.

The foundation is complex.

### Assessment
Minor for foundation. Advisor Experience, Clippy and Decision Clarity principles exist to hide complexity behind clear decisions.


### Elementos Ya Cerrados

1. Universal Production Events.

Closed.

Production Events are universal facts. They do not encode carrier, channel, contest, compensation or career interpretation.


2. Rule Pack interpretation.

Closed.

Rule Packs interpret facts. Forge Core does not hardcode commercial interpretation.


3. Identity model.

Closed.

CommercialPerson handles durable human identity.
CommercialRole handles time-bounded roles.
CommercialAccount handles family, business, corporate and household contexts.


4. Assignment vs Attribution vs Servicing.

Closed.

CommercialAssignment handles formal responsibility.
CommercialAttribution handles credit, origin and split.
CommercialServicing handles operational attention.


5. Evidence and Provenance.

Closed.

Forge can explain where a datum came from, how it was transformed, who reported it, what evidence supports it and what confidence applies.


6. Operational clocks.

Closed.

Event Time.
Effective Time.
Reporting Time.
Evaluation Time.
Payment Time.
Correction Time.

These are sufficient to explain late events, corrections, index lag, payment lag and retroactive changes.


7. PeriodSnapshot.

Closed.

PeriodSnapshot is the universal mechanism for preserving time-bounded evaluation context.


8. Metrics ownership.

Closed.

Every metric must have one conceptual owner.
Other domains consume snapshots and do not recalculate.


9. RuleSnapshot.

Closed.

RuleSnapshot preserves the exact rule context used for a historical interpretation.


10. Rule Pack hierarchy.

Closed.

Carrier.
Distribution Channel.
Rule Pack.
Rules.


11. Commercial Events Taxonomy.

Closed.

Fact Events.
Interpretation Events.
Decision Events.
Payment Events.
Correction Events.
System Events.
Experience Events.


12. Historical explanation requirements.

Closed.

The foundation can explain why something happened, why something was interpreted, why something was paid, why something changed and why something was corrected.


13. Advisor Experience dependency boundary.

Closed.

Advisor Experience consumes official metrics, snapshots and Rule Pack interpretations. It does not own business rules.


14. Economic Motivation boundary.

Closed.

Economic Motivation explains money earned, potential or at risk. It does not own or recalculate source metrics.


15. Command OS dependency boundary.

Closed.

Command OS executes actions over canonical entities and active context. It does not own business interpretation.


### Elementos Que Deben Reabrirse

None.

No foundational element must be reopened.

There are governance obligations, but they do not require changing the foundation.

The foundation is sufficient.


### Consistency Review

Commercial Events vs Metrics

Pass.

Events record what happened or what was interpreted.
Metrics are values owned by domains or Rule Packs.
A metric must not pretend to be an event.
An event must not pretend to be a metric.


Commercial Events vs Rule Packs

Pass.

Production Events are universal.
Rule Packs interpret Production Events.
Interpretation Events can be scoped to a Rule Pack.


Metrics vs Rule Packs

Pass.

Core owns metric contracts and ownership discipline.
Rule Packs define carrier/channel-specific metrics.

### Example

Core may support ruled contest metrics.
SMNYL Agency 2026 may define Prima Meta.


Periods vs Rule Packs

Pass.

Core supports universal clocks and PeriodSnapshots.
Rule Packs define which periods matter for specific interpretation.

### Example

Core supports Evaluation Time.
SMNYL Agency 2026 may define semester evaluation for a specific program.


Evidence vs Rule Packs

Pass.

Rule Packs can be built from official company documents. Evidence and Provenance preserve document source, extraction path, confidence and correction history.


RuleSnapshot vs Rule Packs

Pass.

RuleSnapshot must include carrier, distribution channel, rule pack, rule pack version, rule family, source document and effective dates.


Foundation vs operational agency artifacts

Pass.

The operational agency artifacts do not break the foundation because they are not Core.

They are source material for Rule Pack construction, evidence, operational events, planning contexts and interpretation rules.


### Hidden Dependencies Found

1. Rule Pack identity must be present in every rule-based output.

### Status
Covered by Rule Snapshot Hardening plus Rule Pack constitutional boundary.


2. Operational documents require Evidence and Provenance.

### Status
Covered.


3. Recruitment materials require activity and evidence but not hardcoded Core rules.

### Status
Covered.


4. Partner planning requires assignment, attribution, periods and Rule Pack context.

### Status
Covered.


5. Productivity files require metric ownership discipline.

### Status
Covered.


6. One Thing requires Advisor Experience or productivity interpretation but must not become Core logic.

### Status
Covered.


7. P200 requires relationship, recruitment/revenue context and Rule Pack interpretation.

### Status
Covered.


8. Precont requires recruitment/career/precontract periods and Rule Pack rules.

### Status
Covered.


### Supuestos Peligrosos Eliminados

1. SMNYL terms are universal.

Eliminated.

They belong to SMNYL Agency 2026 Rule Pack.


2. Contest logic belongs in Core.

Eliminated.

Core supports contest interpretation mechanisms. Rule Packs define contest rules.


3. Compensation logic belongs in Core.

Eliminated.

Core supports compensation interpretation mechanisms. Rule Packs define carrier/channel compensation rules.


4. Career paths are universal.

Eliminated.

Core supports career timeline and role transitions. Rule Packs define carrier/channel-specific career rules.


5. Productivity has one meaning.

Eliminated.

Productivity may be a Rule Pack KPI, a manager metric, or behavior signal depending on owner and context.


6. A metric can be recalculated by consumers.

Eliminated.

One owner. Consumers use snapshots.


7. Event date is enough.

Eliminated.

Forge needs Event Time, Effective Time, Reporting Time, Evaluation Time, Payment Time and Correction Time.


8. Evidence is optional.

Eliminated.

Decision-grade facts and rules require evidence/provenance.


### Acoplamientos Indebidos Remaining

None at foundation level.

Potential future coupling risks remain if builders ignore the foundation, but the foundation itself separates:

Core from Rule Packs.
Fact from interpretation.
Assignment from attribution.
Servicing from ownership.
Metrics from events.
Rules from metrics.
Evidence from conclusion.
Forecast from confirmed income.


### Architectural Gaps

No lock-blocking architectural gaps remain.

The foundation does not need a new primitive to support the listed future branches.

### Compensation Intelligence can use

### Partner Intelligence can use

### Productivity Intelligence can use

### Recommendation Final

Declare Foundation Lock Closed.

### Reason

### The foundation now answers the required universal questions

Who is involved?
What account or relationship is involved?
Who was assigned?
Who was credited?
Who serviced?
What happened?
When did it happen?
When did it count?
When was it reported?
When was it evaluated?
When was it paid?
When was it corrected?
What evidence supports it?
What source produced it?
What transformed it?
What rule interpreted it?
What Rule Pack owned that interpretation?
Who owns the metric?
Who consumes the metric?
What changed historically?
Why was a decision made?

This is sufficient for future branches without reopening the foundation.

Future work will build on the foundation, not modify it.


### ¿se Puede Declarar Oficialmente Foundation Lock Closed?

YES - FOUNDATION LOCK CLOSED


### Why Yes

1. Production Events are universal.

The foundation correctly treats production as fact, not interpretation.


2. Rule Packs interpret facts.

The final constitutional boundary resolves the previous blocker.


3. Forge Core remains independent.

### Forge Core no longer assumes

carrier.
distribution channel.
contest.
compensation.
career.
promotion.
KPI.
activity.
recognition.


4. SMNYL Agency 2026 is isolated.

SMNYL Agency 2026 can be the first validated Rule Pack without contaminating Core.

It is source material and rule content.
It is not Forge.


5. Operational agency files are supported.

Planeación Trimestral Partners, Reclutamiento, MP2, MP1B, MP1C, RTW, PM, Precont, P200, One Thing and Resumen can be represented as:

evidence;
source documents;
rule pack inputs;
operational planning artifacts;
activity definitions;
recruitment rules;
productivity rules;
partner planning rules;
experience context;
metrics or snapshots owned by the relevant Rule Pack/domain.

They do not require a foundation redesign.


6. Historical explanation is supported.

### Forge can explain future historical questions using

Production Events.
RuleSnapshots.
Rule Pack snapshots.
PeriodSnapshots.
Evidence.
Provenance.
Attribution.
Assignments.
Servicing.
Metric snapshots.
Correction events.


7. Future intelligence branches are unblocked.

### The foundation supports

Recruitment Intelligence.
Career Intelligence.
Contest Intelligence.
Compensation Intelligence.
Partner Intelligence.
Productivity Intelligence.
Manager Intelligence.

No future branch listed requires a new foundational primitive.


8. Remaining risks are governance risks.

The remaining risks are about discipline in using the foundation, not about missing foundation architecture.

### Examples

Do not hardcode SMNYL in Core.
Do not let UI calculate metrics.
Do not bypass Rule Packs.
Do not show unofficial metrics.
Do not erase historical evidence.
Do not collapse event categories.

These are enforcement responsibilities, not foundation blockers.


### Final Statement

Forge Foundation Lock can be declared closed.

The conceptual foundation is sufficient to support the next generation of Forge intelligence domains without reopening the foundation.

The Core is universal.

Rule Packs carry company, channel, contest, compensation, career, promotion, KPI, activity and recognition specificity.

SMNYL Agency 2026 is the first validated Rule Pack.

SMNYL Agency 2026 is not Forge Core.

YES - FOUNDATION LOCK CLOSED



===== FORGE_CONSTITUTION_AMENDMENT_v1.1.md =====

# FORGE CONSTITUTION AMENDMENT v1.1

## Repository References

- [FORGE_MASTER_BUILD_TREE.md](FORGE_MASTER_BUILD_TREE.md)
- [AGENTS.md](AGENTS.md)
- [FORGE_CONSTITUTION_V3.md](FORGE_CONSTITUTION_V3.md)
- [FORGE_FOUNDATION_LOCK.md](FORGE_FOUNDATION_LOCK.md)

---


### Status
Proposed constitutional amendment.

### Mode
Principal Architect.
Constitutional Reviewer.
Product Philosopher.

### Scope
This document formalizes architectural, product and philosophical discoveries from the Foundation Lock Review, Shared Commercial Model, Compensation Intelligence Discovery, Advisor Experience Discovery, Forecast Intelligence Discovery and Business Planning Intelligence Discovery.

This document does not create code.
This document does not create engines.
This document does not create schemas.
This document does not modify UI.
This document does not modify the Build Tree.
This document does not modify the Roadmap.
This document does not commit changes.


## 1. Executive Summary

Forge OS exists to build the best advisor for advisors.

The Foundation Lock process clarified that Forge cannot achieve that vision if it behaves like a CRM, a report viewer, an onboarding checklist, a dashboard collection or a passive analytics tool.

Forge must become the operational intelligence layer where commercial work happens, where facts are captured once, where rules interpret facts without contaminating Core, where forecasts remain suggestions, where economic impact is explicit, where planning becomes executable, and where the system develops the advisor's judgment over time.

### This amendment introduces eight constitutional principles

1. Capture Once Principle.
2. Forecasts Are Suggestions, Facts Are Facts.
3. Business Planning Principle.
4. Economic Clarity Extension.
5. Causal Clarity Principle.
6. Learning Through Reasoning Principle.
7. Advisor Development Principle.
8. Rule Pack Separation Principle.

These principles do not replace the existing Constitution.

### They strengthen the current constitutional foundation

Advisor First.
Decision Clarity First.
Value Before Work.
Learning By Doing.
Economic Clarity.
Production Events Principle.
No Invented Data.
Rule-Based Transparency.
The Best Advisor for Advisors.

### The central shift is this

Forge must not only show information.
Forge must convert work into intelligence, intelligence into decisions, decisions into actions, and actions into developed commercial judgment.


## 2. Constitutional Context

### The prior Constitution established Forge as

A Decision Intelligence System.
A Career Intelligence System.
A Sales Operating System.
Advisor-first.
Manager-aware.
Action-oriented.
Evidence-disciplined.
Offline-first.
Deterministic at the Core.
AI-assisted only for explanation, language and support.

The Foundation Lock Review added a critical architectural boundary:

Forge Core is universal.
Rule Packs interpret commercial events.
SMNYL Agency 2026 is the first validated Rule Pack.
SMNYL Agency 2026 is not Forge Core.

This distinction prevents company-specific rules from contaminating the system's universal primitives.

The Shared Commercial Model established that Forge must share a single commercial language across domains:

CommercialPerson.
CommercialAccount.
CommercialRole.
CommercialAssignment.
CommercialAttribution.
CommercialServicing.
Policy.
Product.
ProductionEvent.
RuleSnapshot.
PeriodSnapshot.
MetricSnapshot.
Evidence.
Provenance.
SourceSystem.

### The Compensation Intelligence Discovery clarified that

Production Events are facts.
Compensation, Contest, Career, Conservation and Manager Intelligence are rule-based interpretations.
Economic value must be explained without inventing money.

### The Advisor Experience Discovery clarified that

Adoption is a domain-level concern.
The first experience matters.
Help must be contextual and non-invasive.
Learning must be measured by behavior, not exposure.
The advisor must feel that Forge is not another CRM.

The Forecast Intelligence and Business Planning discoveries clarified that:

Forecasts are decision aids, not facts.
Plans must become executable.
Targets without action paths are incomplete.
Gaps must be translated into concrete commercial moves.

This amendment formalizes those discoveries as constitutional principles.


3. AMENDMENT v1.1

The Forge Constitution is amended to include the following principles as official constitutional doctrine.

These principles are binding on future architecture, product design, domain modeling, rule interpretation, user experience, reporting, intelligence outputs and prioritization.

Every future Forge domain must be evaluated against them.

The principles are not implementation instructions.
They are architectural and product constraints.

They define what Forge must become and what Forge must never become.


## 4. Principle 1: Capture Once Principle

### Statement

Forge must become the primary operational source.

No user should capture the same data twice.

If Forge can infer, import, extract or derive a reliable data point, Forge must not ask the user to manually capture it again.

Excel files, PDFs, institutional formats, spreadsheets and reports are derived views.
They are not the primary system of record.

The user should work in Forge.
Forge should generate the reports, exports and documents that the business requires.

### Purpose

The purpose of Capture Once is to prevent Forge from becoming another administrative burden.

If Forge asks advisors, managers or partners to re-enter data already available somewhere else, Forge becomes part of the operational problem instead of solving it.

Forge must reduce friction, not multiply it.

The operating system should capture the commercial fact once, preserve evidence, attach provenance, and allow every domain to consume the same trusted source.

### Benefits

Reduces duplicate work.
Improves data consistency.
Increases advisor adoption.
Reduces operational fatigue.
Improves confidence in outputs.
Makes reporting a byproduct of real work.
Allows managers to trust the same facts advisors use.
Allows Rule Packs to interpret consistent events.
Prevents Excel from becoming a competing source of truth.

### Architectural implications

Forge must distinguish primary operational facts from derived reports.

Production Events, Relationship Events, Assignment Events, Attribution Events and Policy Events should be treated as operational facts when supported by sufficient evidence and provenance.

Reports should be generated from canonical events, metrics, snapshots and Rule Pack interpretations.

### Manual capture is allowed only when

The data cannot be inferred, imported, extracted or derived reliably.
The user is the only credible source.
The captured data has a clear decision or action purpose.
The system can explain why it needs the input.

### Forge must prefer

Import over re-entry.
OCR over manual transcription when confidence is sufficient.
Derivation over repeated capture.
Evidence-backed correction over silent overwrite.
Generated reports over external spreadsheet workflows.

### Risks of noncompliance

Forge becomes a CRM with better language.
Users abandon the system because it creates extra work.
Multiple versions of the truth appear.
Reports diverge from operations.
Managers ask for one version, advisors work from another.
Forecasts and compensation explanations become inconsistent.
Rule Pack outputs become unreliable because input facts are duplicated.

### Constitutional test

Before asking a user to capture data, Forge must answer:

Can Forge already know this?
Can Forge infer this?
Can Forge import this?
Can Forge extract this from evidence?
Can Forge derive this from existing facts?
Does this input produce a decision, action or economic explanation?

If the answer is no, the capture request should be rejected or deferred.


### 5. Principle 2: Forecasts Are Suggestions, Facts Are Facts

### Statement

Forge must clearly separate facts, metrics, forecasts, interpretations and recommendations.

A forecast helps the advisor make a decision.
It is not a guarantee.
It is not a confirmed outcome.
It is not a payment.
It is not production.
It is not a qualification.

Forge must never present a prediction as if it were a fact.

### Purpose

The purpose of this principle is to protect trust.

Advisors and managers may act on Forge outputs. If Forge blurs the line between confirmed facts and possible futures, users can make bad decisions while believing the system has certainty.

Forecast Intelligence exists to improve planning and decision-making, not to manufacture certainty.

### Benefits

Preserves user trust.
Prevents false certainty.
Improves planning discipline.
Protects Economic Motivation from overpromising.
Separates confirmed income from potential income.
Separates official qualification from projected qualification.
Makes uncertainty visible and actionable.

### Guardrails

Every forecast must be labeled as forecast, estimate, scenario or probability.

### Forge must distinguish

Confirmed fact.
Official metric.
Rule-based interpretation.
Forecasted outcome.
Recommended action.
Assumption.

### Forecasts must show their basis when possible

Historical performance.
Current pipeline.
Activity pattern.
Behavior signals.
Rule Pack interpretation.
Period context.
Evidence quality.
Confidence.

### Forecasts must not be used as

Confirmed production.
Confirmed income.
Confirmed commission.
Confirmed contest qualification.
Confirmed conservation result.
Official manager compensation.

### Implications for Forecast Intelligence

Forecast Intelligence must consume official facts, metrics, Rule Snapshots, Period Snapshots and Evidence.

It must not own canonical production metrics.
It must not own compensation results.
It must not own contest qualification.
It must not overwrite official domain outputs.

### Forecast Intelligence may produce

Forecast scenarios.
Risk ranges.
Expected gap.
Likely outcome.
Decision alternatives.
Recommended next action.

Forecast Intelligence must always preserve the difference between:

What happened.
What is currently true.
What may happen.
What Forge recommends doing.

### Constitutional test

If a user could mistake the output for a confirmed fact, the output violates this principle.


## 6. Principle 3: Business Planning Principle

### Statement

Forge must convert goals into executable plans.

Forge must not merely display objectives.

### Forge should transform

Goal.
Forecast.
Gap.
Actions.

Planning must be based on historical performance, current pipeline, installed capacity, observed behavior and active rules.

Planning must not be based on arbitrary estimates.

### Purpose

The purpose of Business Planning is to make commercial ambition operational.

A goal without a plan is pressure.
A plan without evidence is fantasy.
A plan without action is a report.

Forge must help advisors and managers understand what goal they are pursuing, what the current forecast suggests, what gap exists, and what actions can reduce that gap.

### Benefits

Converts aspiration into execution.
Connects daily behavior to monthly and quarterly outcomes.
Improves manager coaching.
Improves advisor autonomy.
Prevents planning from living only in spreadsheets.
Makes gaps actionable instead of discouraging.
Links Mick behavior signals to commercial outcomes.
Creates a practical bridge between revenue, career, contest, compensation and conservation.

### Relationship with Forecast Intelligence

Forecast Intelligence estimates likely outcomes based on available evidence.

Business Planning uses those forecasts to identify gaps and translate them into action paths.

### Forecast Intelligence answers

What is likely to happen?
What may happen under different scenarios?
What risks exist?

### Business Planning answers

What must change?
What action should happen?
Which gap matters most?
What plan is realistic given capacity and rules?

### Relationship with Mick

Mick measures behavior, discipline, consistency and execution.

Business Planning must not treat behavior as decoration.

If a plan requires more meetings, follow-ups, referrals, reviews, calls or prospecting activity, Mick provides the observed behavior context needed to judge feasibility.

A plan that ignores behavior is incomplete.

### Business Planning should therefore consider

What the advisor has done.
What the advisor can realistically sustain.
Where the advisor is inconsistent.
Which behavior bottleneck limits the plan.
Which action rhythm is required to close the gap.

### Constitutional test

### Any planning output must answer

What is the goal?
What is the current forecast?
What is the gap?
What action can reduce the gap?
What evidence supports this plan?
What uncertainty remains?


## 7. Principle 4: Economic Clarity Extension

### Statement

Every relevant commercial gap should be translatable into economic impact when sufficient evidence exists.

### Forge should explain

Income potential.
Expected income.
Income at risk.

Forge must never invent values.

Uncertainty must be shown explicitly.

### Purpose

The purpose of Economic Clarity Extension is to make commercial decisions financially legible.

Advisors do not only need to know that they are missing two policies, a premium amount, a follow-up or a qualification threshold.

They need to understand why that gap matters economically.

Forge should help the advisor see the financial consequence of action or inaction without exaggerating certainty.

### Benefits

Improves motivation through clarity, not hype.
Connects activity to income.
Makes compensation rules understandable.
Makes contest and career gaps economically meaningful.
Helps managers coach with concrete stakes.
Helps advisors prioritize the highest-impact action.
Supports Advisor First decision-making.

### Limits

Forge may translate gaps into money only when it has enough evidence.

### Required evidence may include

Official production facts.
Policy status.
Product context.
Rule Pack.
Rule Snapshot.
Period Snapshot.
Attribution context.
Compensation rules.
Contest rules.
Forecast confidence when using expected income.

### Forge must not create economic estimates from

Unknown commission schedules.
Unknown product rules.
Missing premiums.
Unverified policy status.
Unconfirmed attribution.
Unofficial manager assumptions.
Forecasts presented as facts.

### Guardrails

Income already paid must be separated from income accrued.
Income accrued must be separated from income expected.
Income expected must be separated from income potential.
Income potential must be separated from income at risk.

When uncertainty exists, Forge must say so.

### Valid language

"Estimated."
"Expected based on current evidence."
"Potential if current assumptions hold."
"At risk if this policy does not persist."
"Unknown because the commission rule is missing."

### Invalid language

"Guaranteed" when not confirmed.
"Earned" when only forecasted.
"Paid" when only calculated.
"Qualified" when only projected.

### Constitutional test

If Forge cannot explain the evidence and rule basis for a financial statement, Forge must not present the statement as economic truth.


## 8. Principle 5: Causal Clarity Principle

### Statement

Forge must not only recommend actions.

Whenever possible, Forge must explain the causal chain that connects an action to an outcome.

Forge should teach the advisor why the recommendation matters.

Forge should develop commercial judgment, not only guide isolated decisions.

### Example causal chain

2 policies.
Prima Meta.
Qualification.
Bonus.
Income.

### Purpose

The purpose of Causal Clarity is to make Forge educational without becoming a tutorial.

The advisor should not become dependent on black-box recommendations.

### The advisor should gradually understand the commercial logic

Why this action matters.
Which metric it affects.
Which rule interprets it.
Which period evaluates it.
Which economic outcome depends on it.
Which risk could block it.

### Benefits

Develops commercial judgment.
Improves trust.
Reduces blind compliance.
Helps advisors prioritize.
Improves manager coaching.
Makes compensation and contest logic explainable.
Supports Learning Through Reasoning.
Turns Forge into a development system, not only a recommendation engine.

### Implications for Advisor Experience

Advisor Experience should reveal causal explanations progressively.

Benvenù should not overwhelm the advisor with rules, but it may show a simple causal path from current situation to first value.

Clippy should explain causal chains only when context makes them useful.

Candy Crush Experience should adjust causal complexity to the advisor's current understanding.

### Feature Learning State should distinguish between

User saw the metric.
User used the metric.
User understood the implication.
User acted correctly without help.

### Implications for Manager Intelligence

Manager Intelligence should explain not only who is behind, but why.

### Manager outputs should connect

Behavior.
Pipeline.
Production.
Rule interpretation.
Economic consequence.
Development need.

Managers should be able to coach the causal bottleneck, not only react to the final result.

### Constitutional test

### Every meaningful recommendation should be able to answer

What action?
What metric changes?
What rule interprets it?
What outcome is affected?
What economic impact may follow?
What uncertainty remains?


## 9. Principle 6: Learning Through Reasoning Principle

### Statement

Reading does not mean learning.

Understanding means learning.

Forge must favor comprehension, reflection and reasoning over passive consumption of information.

Learning must be measured by observable behavior and observable understanding, not by exposure.

### Purpose

The purpose of Learning Through Reasoning is to prevent Forge from becoming a knowledge base disguised as an operating system.

Advisors do not become better because they read a screen.
They become better when they understand a situation, make a better decision, execute a better action and can repeat the reasoning with less help.

### Benefits

Improves adoption.
Reduces dependence on training.
Supports progressive mastery.
Makes Clippy quieter over time.
Gives managers better development signals.
Improves advisor confidence.
Prevents superficial completion metrics.

### Relationship with Clippy

Clippy must not measure learning by whether a user dismissed help.

Dismissal is not learning.
Viewing is not learning.
Clicking is not learning.

Clippy should reduce help when behavior shows that the advisor can complete the relevant action with correct understanding and without unnecessary guidance.

### Relationship with Advisor Experience

Advisor Experience owns progressive discovery and feature learning state.

### It should treat learning as a progression

Unseen.
Introduced.
Tried.
Completed with help.
Completed without help.
Learned.
Needs refresh.
Suppressed.

The Constitution now clarifies that the deeper signal is not screen exposure.
The deeper signal is reasoning demonstrated through action.

### Relationship with Candy Crush Experience

Candy Crush Experience should adapt difficulty based on demonstrated understanding.

When the advisor is confused, Forge should simplify the explanation or reduce complexity.

When the advisor demonstrates mastery, Forge should increase the quality of reasoning expected.

Forge must not confuse comfort with learning.
Forge must not confuse struggle with growth.

### Constitutional test

An advisor has not learned because a screen was shown.

An advisor has learned when behavior and reasoning indicate that they can make or execute the decision with less support.


## 10. Principle 7: Advisor Development Principle

### Statement

Forge must not only produce better outcomes.

Forge must help develop better advisors, managers and partners.

The intelligence of the system should transfer progressively to the user.

The final objective is not dependency.
The final objective is growth.

### Purpose

The purpose of Advisor Development is to align Forge's intelligence with human capability.

If Forge only tells users what to do, it may improve short-term execution while weakening long-term judgment.

Forge should help users internalize commercial reasoning, improve behavior, recognize patterns and become more capable over time.

### Benefits

Improves long-term advisor quality.
Improves manager effectiveness.
Improves partner development.
Reduces dependence on blind recommendations.
Creates durable commercial capability.
Supports career growth.
Aligns with the vision of accompanying the full commercial career.

### Risks

Forge could become paternalistic.
Forge could over-coach.
Forge could interrupt work in the name of development.
Forge could mistake activity for growth.
Forge could create dependency if it hides reasoning.
Forge could overload new advisors with advanced logic too early.

### Implications for Mick

Mick must remain Behavior Intelligence.

Mick should not become a motivational module.
Mick should not merely celebrate results.
Mick should measure the actions, habits, consistency and coachability that produce commercial outcomes.

Under this principle, Mick also becomes a critical development signal:

Which behavior is improving?
Which behavior is blocking production?
Which action is repeated without quality?
Which advisor needs simpler guidance?
Which advisor is ready for higher complexity?
Which manager intervention may develop capability?

Advisor Development does not mean Forge replaces the manager.

It means Forge gives the advisor and manager clearer evidence about what must be developed.

### Constitutional test

If an output improves a result while preventing the user from understanding or improving, the output is incomplete.

Forge should guide action and grow judgment.


## 11. Principle 8: Rule Pack Separation Principle

### Statement

Forge Core contains universal primitives.

Rule Packs contain interpretations specific to a carrier, distribution channel, commercial model, contest, compensation plan, career system, promotion path, KPI framework, activity model or recognition structure.

Business rules must not contaminate the universal primitives of Forge Core.

SMNYL Agency 2026 is the first validated Rule Pack.
It is not Forge Core.

### Purpose

The purpose of Rule Pack Separation is to preserve Forge as a universal commercial operating system.

If company-specific rules enter Core, Forge becomes a custom implementation rather than a reusable platform.

Forge Core must understand that commercial events exist.
It must not assume what those events mean under a specific carrier, channel or contest.

### Benefits

Protects universality.
Supports multiple carriers.
Supports multiple distribution channels.
Supports future rule changes.
Protects historical explanations.
Allows SMNYL Agency 2026 to be validated without becoming the system.
Prevents compensation, contest or career logic from leaking into Core.
Allows Rule Packs to evolve without modifying universal primitives.

### Architectural implications

### Forge Core may define

CommercialPerson.
CommercialAccount.
CommercialRole.
CommercialAssignment.
CommercialAttribution.
CommercialServicing.
Policy.
Product.
ProductionEvent.
RelationshipEvent.
RuleSnapshot.
PeriodSnapshot.
MetricSnapshot.
Evidence.
Provenance.
SourceSystem.

### Forge Core must not hardcode

Carrier-specific bonuses.
Contest groups.
Career stages specific to a company.
Promotion criteria.
Compensation formulas.
Conservation formulas.
Recognition rules.
Activity targets.
KPI names specific to a channel.
Agency-specific abbreviations.

### Rule Packs may define

Carrier.
Distribution channel.
Rule Pack identity.
Rule Pack version.
Rule scope.
Rule language.
Rule effective period.
Rule source evidence.
Eligibility rules.
Qualification rules.
Calculation rules.
Attribution rules.
Contest rules.
Compensation rules.
Career rules.
Manager compensation rules.
Recognition rules.
Activity rules.

### Long-term impact

### This principle allows Forge to support

SMNYL Agency 2026.
SMNYL Personal Lines.
AXA Agency.
GNP Agency.
MetLife Agency.
Future carriers.
Future distribution channels.
Future commercial models.

Without modifying Core.

### Constitutional test

If a concept only exists because of a carrier, distribution channel, contest, compensation plan or agency document, it belongs in a Rule Pack or Rule Pack interpretation.

It does not belong in Forge Core.


## 12. How These Principles Complement Existing Principles

### Advisor First

Capture Once protects the advisor from duplicate work.
Business Planning gives the advisor executable direction.
Economic Clarity explains why the work matters.
Causal Clarity develops the advisor's judgment.
Advisor Development ensures Forge helps the human improve, not only the system output.

### Decision Clarity First

Forecast separation prevents false certainty.
Business Planning converts decision clarity into action paths.
Causal Clarity explains why the next action matters.
Economic Clarity expresses relevant gaps in money when evidence supports it.

### Value Before Work

Capture Once directly extends Value Before Work.
Forge should ask for work only when the user receives decision value.
If Forge can obtain the data another way, manual capture is unjustified.

### Learning By Doing

Learning Through Reasoning deepens Learning By Doing.
Doing is necessary, but not sufficient.
The advisor must also understand the commercial reasoning behind better action.

### Economic Clarity

Economic Clarity Extension clarifies that economic translation requires evidence, rule basis and uncertainty labels.
It prevents motivational language from becoming financial invention.

### Production Events Principle

Rule Pack Separation strengthens the distinction between facts and interpretations.
Production Events remain universal facts.
Rule Packs interpret them.

### No Invented Data

Forecast separation, Economic Clarity Extension and Rule Pack Separation all reinforce this principle.
Forge must not invent values, products, rules, income, qualification or certainty.

### Benvenu Principle

Business Planning, Capture Once and Advisor Development support the first experience by ensuring the advisor sees value before bureaucracy.
Benvenu should demonstrate that Forge helps the advisor think and act, not merely fill forms.

### Clippy Principle

Learning Through Reasoning defines when help should reduce.
Clippy should disappear when the user demonstrates understanding, not merely when the user dismisses help.

### Candy Crush Experience Principle

Causal Clarity and Learning Through Reasoning provide the substance that adaptive difficulty should adjust.
The system should adapt reasoning depth, commercial challenge and guidance intensity.

### The Best Advisor for Advisors

All eight principles push Forge closer to becoming the best advisor for advisors:

Less duplicate work.
Clearer truth.
Better planning.
Explicit economic impact.
Stronger causal understanding.
Deeper learning.
Long-term human development.
Universal architecture.


## 13. Possible Conflicts

### Conflict 1
Capture Once vs Evidence Quality.

### Risk
Forge may infer or extract data too aggressively to avoid manual capture.

### Resolution
Capture Once does not override evidence and confidence requirements.
If extracted or inferred data is not reliable enough, Forge must request confirmation or mark uncertainty.


### Conflict 2
Economic Clarity vs No Invented Data.

### Risk
Forge may try to motivate advisors by showing money without enough evidence.

### Resolution
Economic impact may be shown only when supported by evidence, rules and confidence.
Uncertainty must be explicit.
Unknown must remain unknown.


### Conflict 3
Forecast Intelligence vs Decision Clarity.

### Risk
Forecasts may appear authoritative and confuse users.

### Resolution
Forecasts must always be labeled as suggestions, estimates or scenarios.
Confirmed facts and forecasts must be visually and semantically distinct in any future product surface.


### Conflict 4
Advisor Development vs Advisor Efficiency.

### Risk
Forge may over-explain and slow the advisor down.

### Resolution
Development must be contextual, progressive and adaptive.
Forge should teach when teaching improves action or judgment.
Forge should stay quiet when the advisor already understands.


### Conflict 5
Rule Pack Separation vs Product Simplicity.

### Risk
Users may not care whether a rule comes from Core or a Rule Pack.

### Resolution
The architecture must preserve the separation even if the user experience hides complexity.
The user can see a simple explanation.
Forge must still know the Rule Pack, Rule Snapshot and evidence behind it.


### Conflict 6
Business Planning vs Manager Control.

### Risk
Managers may want planning to reflect their preferences rather than evidence.

### Resolution
Manager input can be evidence or context, but it must not silently override facts, Rule Packs or official metrics.
Overrides and assumptions must be explicit.


### Conflict 7
Learning Through Reasoning vs Candy Crush Experience.

### Risk
Adaptive difficulty could oversimplify until the advisor stops growing.

### Resolution
Candy Crush Experience must avoid both abandonment and complacency.
It should reduce friction when needed and increase reasoning depth when the advisor is ready.


## 14. Recommendations For Adoption

1. Treat this amendment as constitutional guidance, not implementation scope.

This document should guide future domain design, but it does not authorize code, engines, schemas or UI changes by itself.


2. Keep Forge Core universal.

### Every future document should distinguish

Core primitive.
Rule Pack interpretation.
Domain-owned metric.
Forecast.
Recommendation.
Evidence.


3. Use Capture Once as a product review gate.

Before approving any capture flow, ask:

Is this data already available?
Can it be inferred?
Can it be imported?
Can it be extracted?
Can it be derived?
What decision does it unlock?


4. Require truth labeling in future intelligence outputs.

### Every output should be classifiable as

Fact.
Metric.
Forecast.
Interpretation.
Recommendation.
Assumption.


5. Require economic guardrails for money language.

### Any financial explanation must preserve

Paid.
Accrued.
Expected.
Potential.
At risk.
Unknown.


6. Require causal explanation for major recommendations.

When Forge recommends a commercial action, it should be able to explain the chain between action and outcome.


7. Treat learning as demonstrated capability.

Advisor Experience should not treat views, clicks or dismissed help as proof of learning.


8. Use Mick as a development signal.

Mick should help identify whether execution behavior supports the plan, blocks the plan or requires manager coaching.


9. Preserve Rule Pack evidence.

Every Rule Pack should be traceable to source documentation, effective periods, version, evidence and provenance.


10. Preserve uncertainty.

Uncertainty is not a product weakness.
It is a trust requirement.


## 15. Final Verdict

This amendment should be adopted as Forge Constitution Amendment v1.1.

### Reason

It strengthens the core identity of Forge without changing implementation scope.

It protects the platform from becoming a CRM, a dashboard collection, a spreadsheet wrapper, a forecasting toy, a training portal or a carrier-specific custom system.

### It aligns the architecture with the product philosophy

Forge should not only help advisors know what happened.
Forge should help advisors understand what matters.
Forge should help advisors decide what to do.
Forge should help advisors understand why.
Forge should help advisors grow.

The eight principles are consistent with the existing Constitution and necessary for the next decade of Forge:

Capture Once prevents operational friction.
Forecast separation protects truth.
Business Planning turns goals into execution.
Economic Clarity makes stakes visible.
Causal Clarity develops judgment.
Learning Through Reasoning deepens adoption.
Advisor Development aligns intelligence with human growth.
Rule Pack Separation preserves universality.

### Final constitutional statement

Forge OS is not the place where advisors enter data for someone else's report.

Forge OS is the place where commercial reality becomes decision clarity, decision clarity becomes action, and action becomes professional growth.

### This amendment moves Forge closer to becoming

The best advisor for advisors.

---


### Status
Repository ratification review.

### Mode
Principal Architect.
Repository Maintainer.
Constitutional Custodian.

### Purpose
Consolidate the architectural decisions that are mature enough to become official repository truth.

### Scope
This document does not discover new domains.
This document does not open new PAQs.
This document does not create code.
This document does not create engines.
This document does not create schemas.
This document does not propose implementation.


## 1. Foundation Review

### Reviewed foundation blocks

Shared Commercial Model.
Identity & Attribution.
Evidence & Provenance.
Periods & Operational Clocks.
Metrics Ownership.
Rule Snapshot.
Commercial Events Taxonomy.
Foundation Lock Review.


1.1 Shared Commercial Model

### Status
FOUNDATION LOCK

### Justification
The Shared Commercial Model now defines the universal language required by Forge domains:

CommercialPerson.
CommercialAccount.
CommercialRole.
CommercialAssignment.
CommercialAttribution.
CommercialServicing.
Policy.
Product.
ProductionEvent.
RuleSnapshot.
PeriodSnapshot.
MetricSnapshot.
Evidence.
Provenance.
SourceSystem.

It is mature enough to become the foundation for Recruitment, Career, Contest, Compensation, Conservation, Revenue, Advisor Experience, Manager Intelligence, Partner Intelligence, Productivity Intelligence, Mick and Command OS.

The model is no longer merely exploratory because it survived hardening across identity, attribution, evidence, clocks, metrics, rules and events.


1.2 Identity & Attribution

### Status
FOUNDATION LOCK

### Justification
The model now separates concepts that previously risked collapse:

CommercialPerson is durable identity.
CommercialAccount groups people, families, households or businesses.
CommercialRole describes what a person is in context.
CommercialAssignment describes formal organizational responsibility.
CommercialAttribution describes credit, origin or contribution.
CommercialServicing describes operational care.
PolicyRole describes policy-level participation.
CommercialRelationship describes durable relationships.

This separation is sufficient to support historical changes in manager, office, partner, servicing, origin, connection, development and compensation credit.


1.3 Evidence & Provenance

### Status
FOUNDATION LOCK

### Justification
### Forge now has a conceptual answer to

Where did this data come from?
Who reported it?
What evidence supports it?
How reliable is it?
What transformations did it pass through?
Which rules were applied?

SourceSystem, EvidenceRecord, ProvenanceRecord, Confidence and Truth Model are sufficient foundation primitives.

### This is required for the constitutional principle

Forge does not invent.


1.4 Periods & Operational Clocks

### Status
FOUNDATION LOCK

### Justification
Forge no longer assumes a single clock.

### The model distinguishes

Event Time.
Effective Time.
Reporting Time.
Evaluation Time.
Payment Time.
Correction Time.

### It also preserves separate commercial clocks

Career Month.
Contest Month.
Semester Month.
NP Contest Month.
Policy Age Month.
Policy Year.
Index Reporting Month.
Quarter Month.
Manager Compensation Quarter.
Partner Tenure Semester.
Persistence Month.

This is sufficient to explain late reporting, retroactive corrections, delayed payments, overlapping rule periods and historical evaluation.


1.5 Metrics Ownership

### Status
FOUNDATION LOCK

### Justification
### The rule is now clear

One metric has one conceptual owner.
Other domains consume.
They do not recalculate.

Production Events own raw commercial facts.
Contest Intelligence owns ruled contest metrics.
Compensation Intelligence owns actual compensation events.
Conservation Intelligence owns LIMRA, IGC, persistence and conservation.
Revenue Intelligence owns pipeline and forecast.
Mick owns behavior and execution signals.
Advisor Experience owns learning and baseline experience snapshots, not business metrics.
Economic Motivation owns economic explanation, not metric calculation.

This prevents duplicate calculations and inconsistent truths.


1.6 Rule Snapshot

### Status
FOUNDATION LOCK

### Justification
RuleSnapshot is now conceptually defined as the preserved rule context used to interpret facts.

### It must preserve

Rule identity.
Rule version.
Rule Pack context.
Carrier.
Distribution channel.
Effective dates.
Publication dates.
Expiration dates.
Correction dates.
Scope.
Source evidence.
Provenance.
Historical applicability.

This is sufficient to prevent 2027 rules from rewriting 2026 results.


1.7 Commercial Events Taxonomy

### Status
FOUNDATION LOCK

### Justification
### Forge now distinguishes

Fact Events.
Interpretation Events.
Decision Events.
Payment Events.
Correction Events.
System Events.
Experience Events.

Production Events are facts.
Rule Packs interpret facts.
Compensation, Contest, Career, Conservation and Manager outputs are interpretations, decisions, payments or snapshots depending on context.

Events are no longer used as a catch-all category.


1.8 Foundation Lock Review

### Status
CLOSED

### Justification
### The final review returned

### FOUNDATION LOCK STATUS
PASS

### FOUNDATION SCORE
92 / 100

### Critical blockers
None.

### Final status
YES - FOUNDATION LOCK CLOSED

The remaining risks are governance and discipline risks, not foundation gaps.

# FORGE PHASE TRANSITION

## Repository References

- [FORGE_MASTER_BUILD_TREE.md](FORGE_MASTER_BUILD_TREE.md)
- [AGENTS.md](AGENTS.md)
- [FORGE_CONSTITUTION_V3.md](FORGE_CONSTITUTION_V3.md)

---

FOUNDATION PHASE TO INTELLIGENCE DOMAINS PHASE

### Status
Official architectural phase transition record.

### Mode
Principal Architect.
Repository Maintainer.
Constitutional Custodian.

### Purpose
Document the formal transition of Forge OS from Foundation Phase to Intelligence Domains Phase.

### Scope
This document does not create code.
This document does not create engines.
This document does not create schemas.
This document does not modify implementations.
This document does not open new PAQs.
This document does not propose new domains.


## 1. Executive Summary

### Forge began with a practical commercial problem

Advisors needed a better way to follow up, communicate with prospects, remember what mattered, and take the next right action.

Forge was not born as a CRM.
Forge was not born as an AI platform.
Forge was not born as a dashboard.
Forge was not born as a reporting system.

Forge began as an attempt to solve commercial follow-up, prospect communication, advisor consistency and decision quality.

### The original problem was not

"Where do we store data?"

### The original problem was

"What should the advisor do next, with whom, and why?"

That origin still matters.

As the project evolved, Forge expanded from conversation and relationship support into a broader Sales Operating System and Decision Intelligence System.

Forge discovered that helping advisors sell more requires more than reminders, notes or dashboards.

### It requires

Commercial identity.
Relationship context.
Production facts.
Evidence.
Provenance.
Operational clocks.
Metric ownership.
Rule interpretation.
Compensation clarity.
Forecast separation.
Planning discipline.
Advisor experience.
Behavior intelligence.

### The Foundation Phase existed to answer a necessary question

What must be true underneath Forge so that future intelligence domains can be built without duplicating logic, inventing data, mixing clocks or contaminating Core with carrier-specific rules?

That work is now sufficiently complete.

During the Foundation Phase, Forge achieved:

A Shared Commercial Model.
A hardened identity and attribution model.
An evidence and provenance foundation.
A multi-clock period model.
A metric ownership doctrine.
A RuleSnapshot model.
A commercial events taxonomy.
A formal Rule Pack separation principle.
A Foundation Lock final review.
A Constitution Amendment v1.1 proposal.
A ratification and foundation closure review.

The project is now ready to transition from designing its foundations to building and formalizing intelligence domains on top of them.

### The next phase is

### Intelligence Domains Phase

This does not mean implementation is automatically approved.
It means the conceptual foundation is stable enough that future work should build on it instead of reopening it.

## 3. Constitution Status

### Constitution Status
APPROVED FOR RATIFICATION


3.1 Original principles

### The original Constitution established Forge as

A Sales Operating System.
A Decision Intelligence System.
A Career Intelligence System.
Advisor-first.
Manager-aware.
Action-oriented.
Evidence-disciplined.
Offline-first.
AI-assisted but not AI-dependent.

### Original ratified principles include

Decision Clarity First.
Intelligence Must Lead To Action.
Advisor First.
No Invented Data.
No Invented Products.
No Projections Without Explicit Data.
Economic Clarity.
Learning By Doing.
Production Events Principle.
The Best Advisor for Advisors.

### Status
### Ratified


3.2 Amendment v1.1

The proposed Constitution Amendment v1.1 adds the following principles:

Capture Once Principle.
Forecasts Are Suggestions, Facts Are Facts.
Business Planning Principle.
Economic Clarity Extension.
Causal Clarity Principle.
Learning Through Reasoning Principle.
Advisor Development Principle.
Rule Pack Separation Principle.

### Status
APPROVED FOR RATIFICATION

### Why
These principles consolidate discoveries already proven through Foundation Lock, Advisor Experience, Compensation Intelligence, Forecast Intelligence and Business Planning.


3.3 Capture Once

### Status
APPROVED

### Role
Capture Once extends Value Before Work.

Forge should become the primary operational source.
Users should not capture the same data twice.
Excel, PDFs and reports should be outputs or evidence, not competing systems of record.

### Why it matters
Without Capture Once, Forge risks becoming administrative burden instead of operating system.


3.4 Causal Clarity

### Status
APPROVED

### Role
Causal Clarity requires Forge to explain why an action matters, not only what to do.

### Why it matters
It turns Forge from a recommendation system into a judgment development system.


3.5 Business Planning

### Status
APPROVED

### Role
Business Planning converts ambition into execution.

### The approved chain is

Goal.
Forecast.
Gap.
Actions.

### Why it matters
Targets without action paths create pressure.
Forge should create operational clarity.


3.6 Learning Through Reasoning

### Status
APPROVED

### Role
Learning is not exposure.
Learning is demonstrated understanding and improved behavior.

### Why it matters
It keeps Advisor Experience, Clippy and Candy Crush Experience from becoming superficial onboarding mechanics.


3.7 Rule Pack Separation

### Status
### Ratified By Foundation Lock

### Role
Rule Pack Separation protects Forge Core.

Forge Core is universal.
Rule Packs interpret commercial events.
SMNYL Agency 2026 is the first validated Rule Pack.
SMNYL Agency 2026 is not Forge Core.

### Why it matters
Without this principle, carrier-specific rules would contaminate the platform and make Forge non-universal.


## 4. Major Architectural Discoveries

The Foundation Phase changed Forge's direction through several major discoveries.


4.1 Forge Core is not Rule Pack

### Discovery
Forge Core contains universal primitives.
Rule Packs contain carrier, channel and commercial-model interpretations.

### Why it changed the product
Forge can now support multiple carriers, distribution channels, contests, compensation plans, career systems and recognition models without modifying Core.


4.2 Production Events are Facts

### Discovery
Production Events are commercial facts.
Contest, Compensation, Career, Conservation and Manager Intelligence are interpretations over those facts.

### Why it changed the product
Forge no longer confuses an event with a result.
A paid policy is not a contest qualification.
A commission event is not the same thing as production.
A bonus is an interpreted result, not a raw fact.


4.3 One Metric, One Owner

### Discovery
Every metric needs a single conceptual owner.

### Why it changed the product
Forge avoids inconsistent dashboards, mismatched compensation explanations, duplicate policy counts and competing LIMRA or IGC values.


4.4 Capture Once

### Discovery
Forge must become the place where work happens, not a place where users re-enter work already done elsewhere.

### Why it changed the product
This shifts Forge from a reporting companion to an operational system.
Reports become generated outputs.
Manual capture becomes a last resort.


4.5 Forecasts Are Suggestions, Facts Are Facts

### Discovery
Forecasts can guide decisions, but they cannot be treated as confirmed truth.

### Why it changed the product
This protects trust and prevents future Forecast Intelligence from overstating certainty.


4.6 Goal to Forecast to Gap to Actions

### Discovery
Planning must become executable.

### Why it changed the product
Forge should not merely show goals.
Forge should translate goals into forecasts, gaps and actions.


4.7 Advisor Development over Dashboard Reporting

### Discovery
Forge's goal is not to report performance.
Forge's goal is to develop better advisors, managers and partners.

### Why it changed the product
This raises the bar for every intelligence domain.
A dashboard that does not create better decisions, behavior or judgment is insufficient.


4.8 Causal Clarity

### Discovery
The advisor must understand the causal chain between action and result.

### Why it changed the product
Forge should explain why two policies, a premium gap, a qualification threshold, a bonus or a conservation risk matters.
This converts information into commercial reasoning.


## 5. What Forge Is

### Forge today is

A Sales Operating System.
A Decision Intelligence System.
A Career Intelligence System.
A commercial intelligence platform.
An advisor-first operating layer.
A manager-aware development system.
A rule-interpreted commercial reasoning system.
A system that converts facts into decisions and decisions into action.

### Forge is not

A generic CRM.
A chatbot.
A dashboard collection.
A note-taking system.
A passive reporting tool.
A carrier-specific calculator.
A spreadsheet replacement that only stores rows.
An AI assistant that invents answers.
An OCR tool that extracts numbers without meaning.


5.1 CRM

A CRM stores contacts, notes, tasks and pipeline.

Forge may contain CRM-like information, but it is not defined by storage.

### Forge is defined by decision output

Who should the advisor act on?
Why now?
What should happen next?
What result is at stake?
What rule or evidence supports the recommendation?


5.2 AI Assistant

An AI assistant responds to prompts.

Forge may use generative AI to explain, draft or improve language, but Forge Core must not depend on AI to decide.

Forge decides.
AI explains.


5.3 Dashboard

A dashboard shows metrics.

Forge may display metrics, but it must not stop there.

### Forge must turn metrics into

Meaning.
Decision.
Action.
Economic impact.
Learning.


5.4 Operating System

Forge is an operating system because it becomes the place where commercial work is coordinated.

It connects facts, people, accounts, relationships, policies, activity, evidence, rules, periods, metrics, opportunities and decisions.


5.5 Intelligence Platform

Forge is an intelligence platform because it interprets commercial reality through domain-specific intelligence.

It does not merely collect data.
It reasons over facts, rules, evidence, clocks and context.


5.6 Architectural definition

Forge OS is an advisor-first Sales Operating System and Decision Intelligence Platform that captures commercial reality once, preserves evidence and provenance, applies universal Core primitives, interprets facts through Rule Packs, and converts commercial context into decisions, actions, economic clarity and advisor development.


## 6. Intelligence Domains Phase

### Next Phase
### Intelligence Domains Phase

### Purpose
Build and formalize intelligence domains on top of the closed foundation.

This phase should not reopen foundational primitives without strong evidence.


6.1 Recruitment Intelligence

### Priority
High

### Why it can now be built
Recruitment can use CommercialPerson, CommercialRole, CommercialAssignment, Evidence, Provenance, PeriodSnapshot, RuleSnapshot and Rule Packs.

The foundation supports candidate identity, repeated applications, precontract cycles, manager assignments, office assignments and historical explanation.


6.2 Partner Intelligence

### Priority
High

### Why it can now be built
Partner Intelligence can use attribution, assignment, development, connection, tenure periods, Rule Packs and manager compensation context without collapsing partner into advisor or manager identity.


6.3 Productivity Intelligence

### Priority
High

### Why it can now be built
Productivity can be modeled as a Rule Pack interpretation over activity, production, period and assignment context.

It should not contaminate Core as a universal hardcoded metric.


6.4 Forecast Intelligence

### Priority
High

### Why it can now be built
Forecast Intelligence can consume official facts, metrics, evidence, behavior signals, periods and Rule Pack interpretations.

### The Constitution now clearly states

Forecasts are suggestions.
Facts are facts.


6.5 Business Planning Intelligence

### Priority
High

### Why it can now be built
Business Planning can consume forecasts, goals, gaps, behavior and Rule Pack constraints.

### The approved planning chain is

Goal.
Forecast.
Gap.
Actions.


6.6 Compensation Intelligence

### Priority
High

### Why it can now be built
Compensation Intelligence can interpret production facts through Rule Packs, RuleSnapshots, attribution and payment periods.

It no longer needs to own raw production or contest metrics.


6.7 Conservation Intelligence

### Priority
High

### Why it can now be built
Conservation Intelligence can use Policy Age Month, Persistence Month, Index Reporting Month, evidence, reporting lag and Rule Pack interpretation.

The foundation supports LIMRA, IGC, persistence and conservation without treating them as identical.


6.8 Advisor Experience

### Priority
High

### Why it can now be built
Advisor Experience can consume official domain outputs without owning business metrics.

Benvenu, Clippy, Feature Learning State and Candy Crush Experience now have constitutional support through Value Before Work, Learning By Doing, Learning Through Reasoning, Causal Clarity and Advisor Development.


## 7. Implementation Guidance

The next phase must preserve foundation discipline.

The following should be avoided.


7.1 Do not reopen Foundation Lock without strong evidence

Foundation should not be reopened because a domain feels difficult.

Reopening requires evidence that the foundation cannot explain a real scenario without distortion.


7.2 Do not introduce carrier logic into Forge Core

Carrier-specific terms, contests, rules, compensation formulas, activity targets and recognition models belong in Rule Packs.

Core must remain universal.


7.3 Do not duplicate metrics

Every metric has one conceptual owner.

Domains may consume metrics.
They must not recalculate official metrics they do not own.


7.4 Do not create new owners for existing metrics

If a metric already has an owner, future domains must request or consume that metric.

They must not create parallel truth.


7.5 Do not skip Rule Packs

If a business interpretation depends on carrier, channel, contest, compensation, career, promotion, KPI, activity or recognition rules, it must go through Rule Pack context.


7.6 Do not build dashboards without intelligence

A dashboard is not enough.

### Every surface should move toward

Meaning.
Decision.
Action.
Economic clarity.
Causal understanding.


7.7 Do not confuse forecasts with confirmed outcomes

Forecasts must not be shown as facts.

Predicted income is not paid income.
Projected qualification is not confirmed qualification.
Expected production is not production.


7.8 Do not ask users to capture data Forge can already know

Capture Once should become a product review gate.

Manual capture must be justified by decision value and evidence necessity.


7.9 Do not hide uncertainty

Unknown must remain unknown.

Low confidence must be visible.
Missing evidence must be acknowledged.
Assumptions must be labeled.


7.10 Do not create dependence without development

Forge should guide users and develop their commercial judgment.

The system should transfer reasoning progressively to advisors, managers and partners.

### Begins now

Intelligence Domains Phase.

The next strategic focus is no longer to define the foundation.

The next strategic focus is to build and formalize intelligence domains on top of the foundation:

Recruitment Intelligence.
Partner Intelligence.
Productivity Intelligence.
Forecast Intelligence.
Business Planning Intelligence.
Compensation Intelligence.
Conservation Intelligence.
Advisor Experience.

### Final historical statement

Forge began by trying to solve commercial follow-up and prospect communication.

It evolved into a Sales Operating System because the real problem was larger than reminders.

The real problem was decision quality.

The Foundation Phase gave Forge the universal primitives, clocks, events, evidence, metric ownership and rule interpretation model required to reason safely.

That phase is now closed.

Forge now enters the Intelligence Domains Phase.

From this point forward, the architectural question changes.

### The question is no longer

"What is Forge built on?"

### The question is now

"What intelligence should Forge produce, and how does that intelligence help the advisor decide, act and grow?"

This transition marks the moment Forge stopped designing its foundation and began preparing to build the intelligence that fulfills its constitutional vision:

Build the best advisor for advisors.
